In Lushan, I met Chairman Chiang, Huang Fu, Xiong Shihui, Wang Chonghui, Vice Commander Zhang, and others. Regarding diplomatic matters, I have already talked with Chairman Chiang before. I also accompanied Gu there this time. In addition to listening to Gu's report, I also briefly reported on the situation in Russia and Xinjiang. The date of my return to Russia has not yet been decided. I must go to the Peking Union Medical College Hospital for another physical examination. If my illness is not a problem, I will prepare to return to Russia. However, I still hope that the Central Government will select other capable people to take my place, because I have been abroad for nearly 20 years. I am really tired of foreign life, and there is no one at home to take care of me. It is okay to return to Russia for a short period of service, but I cannot maintain it for a long period of three to five years. The relationship between Japan and Russia is very tense, as reported in the newspapers. The key is still the issue of the Chinese Eastern Railway. I hope that it will not lead to a split. If one side does not use force, it is not very important. If force is used, a major war will break out, and it cannot be contained. The relationship between China and Russia is still good, and there is not much happening in Xinjiang. Since Hitler became president, the relationship between Germany and Italy has not been very tense. The international situation in Europe is tense, and everyone is actively preparing for war. Since the European War to the present, Europeans are immediately frightened at the mention of war, but the governments of various countries are still competing to prepare for war. However, the preparations are not sufficient, and the outbreak of a major war is not yet imminent. The assassination of the Austrian Prime Minister has made the situation very tense. The European War started from Austria that year, and now Europe is facing another change. Austria will become the fuse of a major war. China and Outer Mongolia only have trade in Zhangjiakou. Baotou has long severed relations with Kulun due to inconvenient transportation. When I was in Russia, I proposed that Russia resume trade between Kulun and Baotou. Russia declined, saying that Outer Mongolia is an independent country, and it is only possible if China and Outer Mongolia reach an agreement. I will stay in Qingdao for three to five days and then return west, returning to Jinan, then to Tianjin, and then to Beiping." (6th)

Songjiang Land Tax Embezzlement Case

Finance Department Investigates the Situation

Collection Director Ye Zongcheng Embezzles Over 100,000 Yuan

Detained in the Province for Questioning, Confesses Voluntarily to Repay in Installments

Zhenjiang News: The major case of Ye Zongcheng, the Songjiang collection director, floating and embezzling more than 100,000 yuan in land tax funds, was discovered by the Finance Department. The county was immediately ordered to detain him and was once detained in the province for questioning. He has now been sent back to the county for detention. A reporter learned the truth of the case from relevant parties and recorded it in detail as follows:

Cause of the Embezzlement: In the Punan and Pubei areas of Songjiang, there are tens of thousands of mu of discounted land. In order to take care of the people's difficulties, the Finance Department ordered that land tax be paid at a 40% discount. Later, the county reported to the department that the land was completely barren and could not pay taxes. Therefore, the department did not strictly inquire about it. Unexpectedly, the collection director and others fully collected from the landowners in the area from the 19th year, without any discount. Nothing was reported to the higher authorities. To date, the settlement is no less than 100,000 yuan. At a time when the provincial government is clarifying officialdom, the director dared to engage in such a major fraud, which can be described as daring.

Process of Exposure: Since the scale of the fraud case was so large, it could not be handled by one person alone. Disputes inevitably arose, and someone secretly reported it to the Finance Department. After receiving the news, Director Zhao immediately ordered the county to detain the director and sent personnel to investigate the matter. Che Zhao, the chief of the second section of the county, who was responsible for land tax, did not report a word about this case in advance. His negligence in his duties is obvious, or there may even be collusion in the fraud. The suspicion is very serious, and the county has been ordered to place him under house arrest.

Confession of Embezzlement: After Ye Zongcheng was escorted to the province, Yan Fang immediately sent personnel to interrogate him. The offender confessed to all the allegations and firmly believed that he was solely responsible for everything, and no one else participated. He was willing to fully repay the embezzled funds in installments, paying 50,000 by the end of October and the remaining funds by the end of the lunar year. After receiving the confession, the Finance Department ordered the offender to hand over the funds within a time limit and temporarily sent him back to the county for custody. It is reported that personnel will still be sent to the county for thorough investigation to determine whether there are any colluders. As for the land tax in the area, the investigation in Pubei has been completed, amounting to about 90,000 yuan. The investigation in Punan is still in progress, and the amount is not much, about 10,000 yuan. (6th)

Hurricane Likely to Strike Shanghai

Direction Unchanged, Arrival Expected Today

Ships from Fujian and Zhejiang Taking Temporary Refuge

Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received reports from the observatory stating that at 6:00 AM yesterday, a hurricane was located at 121 degrees East longitude and 26 degrees North latitude. The wind force at the center was 60 nautical miles, and the speed was extremely high, heading northeast. It had already approached the northeastern sea area of Fuzhou. There were also reports of strong cyclones in the East China Sea. Merchant ships sailing in the sea areas of Fujian and Zhejiang received warnings and many had already chosen shelter to prevent accidents. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's 同華轮 telegraphed yesterday that it had sailed to Taichow and anchored to avoid the storm, and would sail again after the hurricane passed. The 温州班轮 廣濟號 coming from 甌 to Shanghai was originally scheduled to enter the port yesterday, but received a hurricane warning en route. For safety, the ship sailed to Shihphu and anchored temporarily, postponing its arrival in Shanghai. The 海晏輪 sailing from Shanghai to 温州 also received a warning and sailed to the same area to take shelter with the 廣濟號. Consequently, all 温州 ferries were delayed by the storm, and arrival would be delayed by at least twenty-four hours. Merchant ships between Fuzhou and Shanghai were also navigating cautiously. The 南華 ferries and others had also chosen locations to anchor, waiting for the storm to pass before sailing to Shanghai. The 大美晚报 reported that in recent days, a hurricane had been lurking near Taiwan, its force particularly severe, causing great anxiety in the Shanghai shipping industry. This morning (the 7th), it showed signs of heading directly for Shanghai. According to the Pudong Observatory and hurricane experts at Xujiahui, the reason for its potential direct approach was that there were low-pressure zones on both sides of Shanghai, so the hurricane, like an angry horse, was being restrained by two reins, unable to move forward. However, there was a risk of the situation changing at any time, in which case the hurricane would turn east and take its usual path. Currently, however, it was still moving north. At 6:00 AM this morning, the center of the hurricane was located at 26 degrees North latitude and 121 degrees East longitude, that is, between Fuzhou and the northern part of Taiwan, in the north of the Taiwan Strait, about 300 miles from Shanghai. The current speed of the hurricane was 8 to 10 miles per hour. If the speed did not change, the direction did not change, and the storm did not dissipate or undergo other changes, then it would blow into Shanghai after noon tomorrow (i.e., today).

Liu Xiang Has Dropped Resignation Plans

Central News Agency reports that Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, returned to Beijing from Lushan a few days ago. On the evening before last, he took the overnight train from Beijing to Shanghai, arriving in Zhenru around 8:00 AM yesterday and transferring to a car to his private residence on West Ames Road for rest. Around 11:00 AM, he went to the Central Bank to work. Around 5:00 PM, he met with reporters from various newspapers and issued the following statement:

Absolutely No Prohibition on Silver Exports

According to Mr. Kong, rumors spread by malicious individuals claimed that the government was about to prohibit the export of silver or impose an export tax on silver, causing widespread panic and a large outflow of silver. In reality, the government has absolutely no intention of prohibiting the export of silver or imposing an export tax on silver. The truth is now clear to most people, and the quantity of silver exports has greatly decreased. It is expected that it will soon be shipped back to China. Mr. Kong also stated that finance is like the blood of the human body. Import and export should be allowed to occur naturally. Drastic measures should not be taken under normal circumstances, as this would damage credibility. However, this does not apply in emergency situations. The current silver reserves in Shanghai are less than 500 million, and about 290 million are held by domestically-owned banks. Therefore, it is hoped that the people will not be overly alarmed about the issue of silver outflow.

Remarkable Achievements in Abolishing Excessive and Miscellaneous Taxes

Mr. Kong continued that since the Ministry of Finance began vigorously abolishing excessive and miscellaneous taxes nationwide on July 1, the achievements have been remarkable, and the burden on people in various regions has been greatly reduced. As for the financial compensation for provinces after the abolition of excessive and miscellaneous taxes, there is actually no need to worry. The increase in excessive and miscellaneous taxes in various provinces and cities was improper in the first place. For example, if a certain provincial government builds a very luxurious building and needs a million dollars, it increases excessive and miscellaneous taxes because the provincial treasury has no funds. Such an improper increase in the burden on the people can certainly be abolished. Therefore, there will definitely be no problem with the financial revenue and expenditure of various provinces after the abolition of excessive and miscellaneous taxes.

Food Transportation and Sales Bureau to be Established Soon

Regarding the preparation of the Ministry of Finance's Food Transportation and Sales Bureau, various sectors have been contacted repeatedly, and it will be established soon. The current progress is that investigations are being conducted separately on the amount of food produced and needed in various regions. After the food purchase is established, it will be distributed based on the disaster situation in various regions. The transportation and sales aspects will be jointly handled with the Railways and Communications Departments. As for the organization of the Trust Bureau, Ye Zhuotang has been appointed as the director. The business scope of the bureau will be to operate trust businesses such as savings and insurance, but it will differ slightly from ordinary trust institutions. Regarding the issue of revising the Banking Savings Law, I have submitted it to the Executive Yuan for discussion in consideration of the difficulties faced by businesses. However, since the law was drafted by the Legislative Yuan and approved and promulgated by the Central Government, whether it can be amended in the future remains to be discussed.

Liu Xiang's Resignation Plans Have Been Dropped

Sichuan Bandit Suppression Commander Liu Xiang had previously requested to resign from the Central Government. Now, after the Central Government sent a telegram to retain him, his resignation plans have been dropped, and he will continue to be responsible for Sichuan's military and political affairs. The Sichuan provincial authorities had previously requested the Central Government to allocate silver bars worth ten million to be shipped to Sichuan as a guarantee for paper money because a large amount of silver was flowing from the inland to the cities, causing the rural economy to decline. The Central Government has approved this, and it will be shipped to Sichuan soon. The rumor that Sichuan requested one million in military funds for bandit suppression is actually a misunderstanding. Regarding the issue of the election of representatives from the four northeastern provinces to the Fifth National Congress, when reporters asked Mr. Kong about this, he replied that the matter should be discussed by the Organization Committee of the Central Party Headquarters. The election of representatives from the four provinces to attend the Fifth National Congress may begin with an investigation into the number of party branches and party members in the four provinces in the past, and then a method of election will be discussed. Whether the representatives will be appointed by the Central Government has not yet been decided.

Planning to Inspect Finances in the Southwest

Mr. Kong has decided to travel to the Southwest during his spare time from official duties to inspect the financial situation of the provinces. He has not been assigned any missions. The date of departure has not yet been decided. Mr. Kong also plans to travel to Sichuan, Gansu, Yunnan, and other provinces after inspecting the Southwest.

Huang Fu Met with Reporters Yesterday Morning

Scheduled to Enter Beijing Next Week

Details of Jiangxi Province's Achievements as an Example for the Country

Restoration of Order in North China Cannot Be Said to Have Made No Progress

Huang Fu, Chairman of the Executive Yuan's Peiping Political Reorganization Committee, went to Lushan last month at the invitation of President Wang and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to discuss political affairs. He returned to Shanghai on the YongSui warship on the evening of the 6th. He met with reporters from various newspapers at his private residence at 10:00 AM yesterday morning.

Issued a Written Statement: "I went to Lushan on the 8th and 10th at the invitation of President Wang and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. I originally planned to return in a week, but Chairman Chiang Kai-shek felt slightly unwell after intense work in the hot summer, so I stayed in Lushan for a while. Now, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's health has fully recovered, and he is personally handling political affairs as usual every day. During this period, I took the opportunity to inspect the bandit suppression work in Jiangxi Province and the political reconstruction after the recovery of the bandit areas. I feel that all the staff of the various agencies are persevering, hardworking, and devoted to their work, handling a large amount of affairs with a very small number of personnel. Therefore, all work is very tense, sweeping away the previous lax atmosphere. This is the most worthy of emulation by public officials in various places. Regarding political affairs in North China, Director Yin is now returning north to resume his duties, and the war zone reorganization issues will soon be addressed one by one. In short, after a major war, the wounds have not yet healed, and the people's strength has been depleted. Reorganizing political affairs and restoring order is not easy. Judging from the current situation, it is certainly not entirely satisfactory, but compared to this time last year, it cannot be said that there has been no progress."

Jiangxi Province Has a Complete System

Mr. Huang then replied to questions from the reporters, stating: "I spent a lot of time in Jiangxi, so I used my spare time to inspect the political situation in the province. Jiangxi Province is a bandit area, and North China is a disaster area, so there are many things that can be observed and emulated. The results of the inspection show that public officials in Jiangxi Province are able to focus on their work. The system in Jiangxi Province has been extensively studied and is now extremely complete. The province's governance is unified, so progress in politics and savings in expenses are evident. I believe that this system is worthy of emulation by all provinces in the country, so I have copied a copy of the province's laws, regulations, and detailed rules for officials in North China to refer to and emulate after I arrive in Peiping."

Reorganization of North China

Regarding various issues in North China, I also discussed them with President Wang and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Lushan. The reorganization of the disaster area will begin, but in terms of environment and reality, the progress is difficult. It should be done step by step. The reorganization of political affairs in North China will also be carried out gradually. Mr. Huang continued that the economic strength of Europe and other countries is much greater than that of China, but even there, the restoration of vitality in war zones has not been rapid.

Returning North in One Week

Mr. Huang continued, "This return to Shanghai is to take care of family matters. I plan to stay for a week, then enter Beijing to visit President Wang, and then return north to resume my duties. As for the rumors that the Sino-Japanese issues in North China are difficult to resolve, this is just speculation. Any issue depends on one's own efforts. For example, if a person has a sore on his hand, the blood cells in his whole body will be mobilized to resist it, and the body will recover."

Ten Thousand Bags

Saigon Rice Arrived in Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday

Prices Continue to Fall in Both Northern and Southern Rice Markets

大公社 reports that the first batch of 100,000 bags of Saigon rice ordered by Shanghai rice merchants and banks for the September term arrived in Shanghai on an foreign ship on the morning of the 6th and were unloaded at the Yangshupu Wharf. Rice merchants and banks that had ordered the rice all went to the managing foreign firms such as 達孚, 泰隆, 公和, etc. yesterday to pick up their goods with their order receipts. September term Saigon rice was valued at $11.7 per bag, calculated at 180 catties per Sima scale. When converted to 150 catties per new Shanghai 市斛, each 石 is only within $10. Therefore, the goods that arrived in Shanghai this time had already been sold. There are still 400,000 bags for the October term, scheduled to be loaded in Shanghai at the end of this month.

Prices Continue to Fall in Both Northern and Southern Rice Markets

The rice boats from various rice merchants arriving at the rice markets in the north and south have been carrying new rice in recent days, and old rice has become relatively scarce. Recently, because there were more reserves of rice in various places, the highest price of rice transported to Shanghai from the interior has fallen to within the $13.5 limit price. The secondary-grade rice is around $12 and $11. After the morning rain in Shanghai yesterday, the prices announced in the market fell again by two or three cents. According to the observation of the rice industry, after all the foreign rice arrives and the late rice comes on the market, the price of rice will definitely experience a special decline.

Jiangxi Province Tribute Rice Shipped Back to Shanghai

Previously, Jiangxi Province experienced a drought and famine this year, and rice prices soared, causing panic among the people. In order to provide relief, the provincial government ordered the Jiangxi Yumin Bank to purchase 10,000 bags of tribute rice in Shanghai and transport them to Nanchang and Jiujiang for flat sales. Now, the province has received a lot of grain from neighboring provinces, and the price has plummeted by about three dollars per dan. However, the price of rice in Shanghai is still strong, so it is planned to ship 5,000 bags of tribute rice stored in Jiujiang to Shanghai for sale in order to regulate the supply and demand of grain. According to Shanghai rice industry sources yesterday, some of the rice has already arrived in Shanghai, and the remaining amount will continue to arrive within the next week.

Telecommunications Personnel Return to Shanghai

The National Telecommunications Conference convened by the Ministry of Communications in Beijing concluded on the 6th. Bao Keyong, Director of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, Yu Runsheng, Chief Engineer, Hua Shijian, Chief of the Reporting Section, Xu Xueyu, Director of the Telephone Bureau, Yu Bingjian, Chief Engineer, and Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, all left Beijing for Shanghai after the closing ceremony.

Eurasia

New Aircraft Scheduled to Fly to Beijing

To be Flown to Beijing for Senior Central Figures to Test Ride

All Staff Held a Gathering Yesterday

-Celebration of Successful Long-Distance Flight to be Held Today-

华东社 reports that a large Junkers JU-52 aircraft recently purchased by the Eurasia Aviation Company had flown from Berlin to Shanghai and is currently staying at the Hongqiao Airport. General Manager Li Jingcong has decided to hold a banquet at the Dadong Hotel at 7:00 PM this afternoon to celebrate the successful flight of pilot Gebelenz, etc. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Gathering

After the aircraft arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, the chief pilot Gebelenz and his party stayed at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund. At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, Mr. Gebelenz and others visited the Eurasia Company. All staff of the company, led by Li Jingcong, held a dinner gathering at the Dadong Hotel on Nanjing Road at 6:00 PM last night. Mr. Li introduced the guests one by one, and there were no outside guests accompanying them.

Celebration to be Held Today

To celebrate Chief Pilot Baron Gebelenz, Deputy Officer翁托特, etc., the company has decided to hold a banquet at the Dadong Hotel at 7:00 PM this afternoon. It is expected that there will be a lively scene.

Flying to Beijing on the 12th

According to Mr. Zha Zhenwu, secretary of the company, the aircraft is still staying at the Hongqiao Airport. Manager Li believes that the aircraft is a novelty in China, so he has decided that Mr. Gebelenz will fly to the capital on the 12th of this month (next Wednesday) and invite senior officials from various ministries and departments of the Central Government to ride the aircraft for a tour around the capital.

Li Jingcong's Remarks

According to Mr. Li Jingcong, today's (the 7th) report on the arrival of the company's new aircraft in Shanghai was not very detailed. The wings of the aircraft are different from ordinary aircraft and are installed under the fuselage. Even when fully loaded with 3,500 kilograms, it only needs to travel 270 meters on the ground to take off when the wind is calm. After taking off, the speed of flight in the air can be increased to 260 kilometers and 300 kilometers per hour with the help of this auxiliary wing. When landing, the speed of flight can be reduced to only 65 kilometers per hour, so even when fully loaded, the aircraft only needs to continue for 180 meters on the ground after the wheels touch the ground to stop completely.

Shanghai-Tianjin Shipping Industry Reaches Agreement

Warning to Fuxin and Fuji

Regarding the Reduction of Freight Charges for the Songshan Maru

新声社 reports that after 21 companies, including the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the privately-run Sanbei Company, implemented cooperation and organized the Shanghai-Tianjin Shipping Association, the British companies Taikoo and Jardine signed agreements with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to join the cooperation. Freight rates and rebates for goods between Shanghai and Tianjin are completely unified and public. Now, the Fuxin Flour Mill, a Chinese company, entrusted the Fuji Customs Brokerage to transport 80,000 bags of flour to Tianjin on the Japanese company Nisshin's Songshan Maru. According to the association's regulations, the freight rate is 18 cents and the handling fee is 14 cents, totaling 32 cents. Today, Nisshin reduced the freight and handling fees to a total of more than 20 cents, which aroused the public anger of Chinese and foreign shipping companies. The member shipping companies of the association decided to hold a meeting yesterday: (1) The Shanghai Shipping Association will send a letter to the Fuxin Flour Mill to warn it; (2) The Shanghai Forwarding and Customs Brokerage Association will send a letter to the Fuji Customs Brokerage to warn it. An emergency meeting is scheduled to be held again today to discuss countermeasures. The situation is very serious.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Four New Ships

Decision to Use Chinese Captains

First Ship Expected to Arrive in Shanghai by the End of October

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's four sea liners being built in the UK, 海元 and 海亨, have been launched. According to a telegram from Wu Daming and others, the deck and other items are being installed. They will not be completed by the middle of this month, so it is estimated that the first ship, 海元, will not be able to leave the UK until after the 20th of this month. The earliest date of arrival in Shanghai is at the end of October. 海亨 will arrive in Shanghai at the beginning of November. The captains of all four new ships have been inquired about in Hong Kong. The Hong Kong Customs has no restrictions on the use of Chinese shipowners for passenger ships as long as they are qualified. Therefore, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has decided with Chief Captain Shen Jiyun and the Ship Department to appoint Chinese captains for the four sea liners. The arrangements are currently being discussed and will be announced next month.

Pan Xulun Returned to Shanghai from Hunan the Day Before Yesterday

Talks About the Progress of Hunan Province's Construction

Hoping for Investment from Financial Circles in Other Provinces

This year, the China Economic Society held its 11th annual meeting in Changsha and also inspected the economic construction of Hunan Province. The Shanghai members of the society who went to the meeting included Pan Xulun, Li Quanshi, Sheng Zhuosan, Tang Qingzeng, Zhuang Zhihuan, Jin Guobao, and more than 20 others. It is learned that Mr. Pan Xulun returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday due to pressing duties. Mr. Pan told visitors yesterday:

"I went to Changsha with my colleagues from the Economic Society to attend the annual meeting and was invited by Chairman He of Hunan Province to visit the new policies and the achievements of social enterprises in the Changsha area. I would like to briefly mention them for the benefit of those who care about provincial administration and entrepreneurs.

Since He Jian, Chairman of Hunan Province, eliminated the communist disaster and presided over Hunan's administration in the spring of 1930, he has been able to gradually bring Hunan Province into a state of peace and order in four or five years. Mr. He has been able to lead by example in political measures and has worked hard to carry out various constructions, so he is deeply loved by the people of Hunan. Although he holds military, political, and party power simultaneously, he feels no officialdom, enters and exits freely, and eliminates escorts. On the one hand, he actively promotes culture, improves education, promotes industry, and conducts statistical surveys. The provincial government has published about 40 or 50 publications on Hunan's statistics, such as the Hunan Yearbook, the Hunan Economic Research Institute Series, the Hunan Population Statistics, the Hunan Price Index, etc. Under the personal promotion of Chairman He, the item of national martial arts has developed very commonly. When we visited the National Martial Arts Club, we saw that the performers included male and female primary and secondary school students, soldiers, and ordinary ladies from all walks of life. Chairman He and the directors also sat among the crowd to watch. Chairman He himself is proficient in national martial arts and entered the arena to perform. Such a civilianized and admired official is a model for military and political authorities. As for the spirit of Hunan's officials at all levels, judging from what I have seen in the past few days, there is very little officialdom. All officials are able to take the lead and operate on their own, which is truly rare.

Hunan Education has always been known for its development. In recent years, Hu Shuhua has been running Hunan University. He only spends 20,000 yuan a month from the province, but the achievements of his departments are better than those of national universities that cost 60,000 to 70,000 yuan a month. As for social education, the degree of development is actually better than that of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, and Shanghai. At the invitation of the Education Department, our company gave public lectures at the Zhongshan Hall in Changsha on economic issues and accounting improvement. Each session was full, with no less than 1,000 to 2,000 people. When our company gave public lectures elsewhere, there were never so many listeners. This shows the high level of education among the general public in Hunan and their special concern for social and economic issues.

According to what Chairman He said about Hunan Province's trade situation, imports exceed exports by as much as 1.8 million yuan per month. The largest items are gasoline and cigarettes, so the way to remedy the excess of imports is to start from here. The Hunan Provincial Industrial Experimental Institute has invented the use of alcohol instead of gasoline, and all public and private groups have risen up to advocate not smoking cigarettes. Everywhere we went, we saw signs on the walls saying "Sorry, no smoking," and government offices and party branches posted "Smoking is prohibited." As a result, in fact, there are far fewer smokers in Hunan Province, and the amount of cigarette imports has greatly decreased in recent years. Hunan is seeking to offset the trade deficit by starting with replacing gasoline and not smoking cigarettes, which has a huge effect. It can be seen that everything only needs to be done practically, and it is not difficult. The most valuable new invention in Changsha's industry is the alcohol car. This matter has been successfully tested by the Provincial Industrial Experimental Institute. By slightly adding special devices to ordinary cars, alcohol can be used instead of gasoline as fuel. During my week-long stay in Changsha, all the cars I rode in burned alcohol. All the situations such as starting, driving, and stopping the car were not inconvenient in the slightest. Two or three years ago, Hunan invented charcoal cars, but using charcoal as fuel was still inconvenient in many ways. The fuel took up too much space on the car, and it was not clean, and it took time to start the fire, and the power was slightly lower. Now, replacing gasoline with alcohol can avoid all difficulties. Now, when my country is developing highways and promoting aviation, the value of importing gasoline in a year is shocking. Hunan can replace gasoline with self-made alcohol, and its importance to the national economy and national defense is difficult to express in words.

In addition to the existing spinning mills and machine factories, the new organizations in Changsha's industry include zinc smelting plants, glass factories, and paper mills, all of which are promoted by the provincial government allocating provincial funds to start them. All glass appliances are very exquisite and are definitely sufficient to resist imported goods with a surplus. As for the paper mill, it has recently started construction, and because of the abundance of nearby raw materials, the results must be good. However, the capital of each factory is small, with the largest being 200,000 and the smallest being 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. With this opportunity to develop industry, I only hope to concentrate the huge amount of funds in Shanghai and invest a small amount of several million yuan in Hunan to manage it, and the public and private sectors will benefit, and the results will be seen immediately. I deeply hope that Shanghai capitalists will pay attention to this opportunity.

In addition, Chairman He has spared no effort in the scenic construction of Hunan Province. The members of our company were invited by the provincial government to visit Mount Heng. Mount Heng is the first scenic spot in Hunan Province. The situation is majestic. The provincial government has set up the Mount Heng Management Bureau to actively engage in road repairs, afforestation, and sorting out famous monuments and historical sites. It has already achieved remarkable results. The mountain is more than 3,000 feet high, and the climate is very cool in summer. It is developed as a summer resort and is comparable to Lushan and Mogan. The annual meeting of our company coincided with the hot summer. As soon as we entered Mount Heng, we felt cool. I think the Yuehan and Yupi railways will be built in the near future. It will only take two days to go to Mount Heng from Shanghai and Guangzhou. At that time, those who go to visit will definitely follow each other."

Railway Bureau Periodically Receives Merchants

Explanation and Observation of Cargo Transportation Procedures

The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Administration plans to cooperate with producers and sellers on the principle of fairness to seek mutual benefit, further extending its effectiveness to regulate supply and demand and develop the national economy. Shanghai is the main center of production and sales. Representatives of various important industries in the city have been invited three times, on August 22 last year, February 8 and July 16 this year, to discuss cooperation. On June 9 this year, they also participated in the China National Products Production and Sales Federation to report on the hope of cooperating with both producers and sellers. Recently, in consideration of various opinions, the general outline of cooperation methods for production, transportation, and sales at stations along the line has been stipulated. One of the provisions is "In places where there are large quantities of goods produced and sold, special personnel will be dispatched to guide or handle transportation procedures." In addition to handling transportation procedures, business offices have been established in Shanghai Jing'an Temple Road, Shiliupu, and Nanjing Taiping Road, specializing in this matter. Other important stations will continue to be established. Regarding the guidance of transportation procedures, although some people have been sent to various places to explain to the industrial and commercial circles and publish regulations for reference, the procedures and calculation of freight are still not easy to understand. In order to solve this difficulty, the railway bureau first contacts important companies, factories, and stores in Shanghai and asks them to send personnel who handle the transportation or equivalent personnel. The railway bureau divides them into several classes to give detailed explanations and on-site observations on all current railway transportation methods and freight calculation methods. The location is at the Shanghai North Station, and there is no charge. The first class is tentatively set at 40 people. The training period is limited to two weeks (from September 17 to 30, except Sundays, from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM every day. At other times, you can still work in various companies, factories, and stores). The railway bureau has sent this plan to various companies, factories, and stores and asked them to notify the selected participants with a letter before September 15.

Cotton Should Be Inspected at the Place of Origin

Statement from Two Cotton Organizations in Hankou

The Hankou Cotton Import Industry Association and the Cotton Firm Industry Association sent a telegram: "To the Legislative Yuan, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, National Economic Committee, and Cotton Control Committee: The malpractice of cotton adulteration is too deep-rooted. To seek elimination, the first thing to do is to treat the root cause. Treating the symptoms instead of the root cause will be a burden on good governance, even with good laws and intentions. In recent years, the government has implemented inspection to improve the status of domestic cotton. The legislation is not very good, but because it has failed to treat the root cause, cotton merchants have suffered greatly for several years, and the effect is very limited. Now, in order to quickly eliminate the malpractice, the Interim Regulations on Prohibiting Cotton Adulteration have been promulgated. The government believes that the implementation of these regulations will eliminate the malpractice and restore the cotton industry. However, the regulations, no matter how strict, will only punish the innocent while the perpetrators will still be at large without any scruples.

New York: Rubber opened with a sharp drop, down 7 to 9 pounds. December futures rebounded 3 pounds, but fell 1 pound at 10:40 AM. March futures also fell 1 pound. Futures trading was very sluggish.

Securities: New York: Before the New York stock market opened, the factors affecting the market were: (1) Government bond prices have now rebounded; (2) The number of shares sold in various stocks, except for mining stocks, has not increased due to yesterday's price drop. The unfavorable factors for the market are the continued lack of construction news, the failure of industrial news to excite people, and the increasingly cautious approach due to the development of the textile strike. When the securities market opened today, trading was scarce, and fluctuations were mixed. Most stock prices fell slightly. Although there were occasional support rallies, sentiment was unsettled. It is expected that the market will remain unstable. New York stock prices are as follows:

Songjiang

Supervisory Committee Member Investigates Land Tax

The Central Supervisory Yuan sent an investigator, Gu Fengxiang, to Songjiang. This morning (the 6th) at 8:00 AM, he went to the county government where County Magistrate Jin Yan received him. It is said that his mission is to investigate land tax in this county, including the conversion of land tax into grain for transport. The investigation was very thorough. He left the county government after several hours of investigation. It is said that Mr. Gu has been in Songjiang for many days, secretly consulting with various parties, for more than a day.

Suzhou: Jin Shuren Recovers from Illness, Case Awaits Trial

Former Xinjiang Province Chairman Jin Shuren, due to being ill while in custody, was sent to Nanjing Central Hospital for treatment with the approval of the Suzhou High Court. He has now recovered. Yesterday (the 7th), the presiding judge of this case at the High Court, Lu Wenlan, ordered the Jiangning District Court to return Jin for trial, so that a date can be set for the continued hearing.

Opium Pill Suspect Arrested in Suzhou

Opium Pill King Li Wenxiang of Wuxi, established an opium pill operation at Dongxin Bridge outside the North Gate of Wuxi. After the case was discovered, Li Wenxiang fled to Suzhou and hid at his relatives' place. The Wuxi Public Security Bureau's Second Sub-bureau learned of this and sent Detective Yu Wensheng to Suzhou to investigate secretly. On the evening of the 6th, Li was arrested at No. 15 Xinxin Hotel outside the Chang Gate and taken to the relevant police district. Yesterday (the 7th), he was transferred to the General Bureau to await Wuxi County to send personnel to Suzhou to escort him back for trial.

Thorough Investigation of Land Tax Fraud

The Wuxian land tax fraud case, which has attracted attention from all parties, has led the Department of Finance to send Committee Member Dong to Suzhou for a secret investigation. The investigation of the unauthorized collection has been completed, and the fraud has been confirmed. The registrar Qian Zhonghua has been placed under surveillance pending investigation. Currently, the investigation of historical arrears and land reclamation is underway. Committee Member Dong is determined to conduct a thorough investigation, so he investigates each household, without minding the trouble. However, Wuxian County has a vast area, with more than 1,040 map divisions, 1.81 million mu of land, and more than 600,000 grain households. It may be impossible to complete the investigation in a short time. A thorough investigation may take three to four months, so it is not known when this case can be concluded. As for the unauthorized collection, the abuses are deeply rooted. A thorough investigation will involve hundreds of people, including the surveyors (i.e., tax collectors) and tax evaders from each map division, which may lead to a major case. Committee Member Dong will go to the provincial capital in the next few days to report the investigation progress to the Department of Finance and request instructions.

Wuxi: Unprecedented Opium Pill Case Cracked

The well-known opium pill manufacturer Wang Guiqing, previously manufactured opium pills on a boat in the Meijing area. The Public Security Bureau's Supervisory Office cracked the case on May 15th of this year, and arrested boatman Zhu Baoshan. The main culprit, Wang Guiqing, escaped and was placed on the wanted list. The day before yesterday morning, the Supervisory Office received a tip-off that Chen Shaokun's house at No. 10 Nanyang Lane inside Guangfu Gate was selling opium pills. Chief Inspector Wang personally led the entire guard team, patrol team, and detective team police officers to search the premises. They found 41 tins of Guo Fusheng Ren Ma Pai, Chen Feng Pai, Yun Long Pai, and red opium pills of various sizes, totaling 37,600 pills, and arrested Chen Shaokun. Together they were taken to the bureau. Section Chief Yi and Chief Inspector Wang interrogated him severely. Chen confessed that these opium pills were supplied by the wanted opium pill manufacturer Wang Guiqing. Chief Inspector Wang then dispatched Inspector Wang Jixiong, leading police officers and Chen Shaokun, to search Wang Guiqing's house at No. 2 Silangjun Lane. They discovered 1,000 Ren Ma Pai opium pills, 100 packets of Kuai Shang Kuai Du pills, one red pill gun, and scattered opium powder, etc. The main culprit, Wang Guiqing, escaped again. At that time, a modern young woman, Chen Yangshi, happened to come to Wuxi from Shanghai to deliver raw materials for opium pills to Wang's house, and was also arrested. She was taken to the bureau along with Wang Guiqing's wife Wang Hushi and maid Hu Qiusi for questioning. Hu Qiusi claimed to live across the street from Wang's house and was mistakenly arrested. Director Chen found Hu Qiusi's expression to be frightened and highly suspicious, so he personally led Chief Inspector Wang and the police team to search Hu Qiusi's house. They found two opium pill manufacturing machines, a box of raw material powder, 4,550 opium pill paper boxes, opium pill trademark printing paper, etc., and arrested Hu Qiusi's landlord, Xue Zhicheng, and took him to the bureau for questioning and detention pending verification. In total, the search lasted for ten hours and ended in the evening. Yesterday, Director Chen of the Public Security Bureau, believing that the house where Wang Guiqing lived belonged to Hou Hongjian, went to the scene with Hou Hongjian at about 1:00 PM to investigate. Unexpectedly, a large number of opium pills, totaling 109,000 pills, were found in the courtyard of the house. Director Chen ordered the driver to return to the bureau and ordered Chief Inspector Wang to lead the police to bring the opium pills to the bureau. He also summoned and ordered the arrest of Chen Shaokun's wife Zhu and Yang Axue, who introduced Wang Guiqing to live in Hou's house. Director Chen offered a reward of 100 yuan to apprehend the fugitive Wang Guiqing.

Bus Overturns Between Xiyi, Many Casualties

The Jiangnan Long-Distance Bus Company's Xichang bus, with 32 passengers, drove from Wuxi to Yixing the day before yesterday afternoon. It drove at full speed all the way until it reached Fude Bridge near Changxing Town, which belongs to Yixing County. By then it was dusk. A dog happened to be walking slowly in the road. Although the driver honked the horn to warn it, it did not move out of the way, so he swerved to avoid it. However, the bus was moving very fast at this time, and the bridge had a wooden railing, which was broken when the bus crashed into it. The bus also overturned into the river. Fortunately, the river water was shallow, but the passengers were shocked by the impact. Seven people were seriously injured and three died on the spot. More than 20 people were slightly injured. Soon, four more of the seven seriously injured died. The rest were sent to Yixing Minsheng, Renxing, and Fanggu hospitals for treatment. When the bus crashed into the river, a woman washing clothes by the river happened to be crushed under the bus and died on the spot with her brains splattered. The stationmaster of Yixing Station rushed to the scene immediately after receiving the news of the accident and got the bus out of the river. The county magistrate Zhong Jingcheng and the chief of the Public Security Bureau also arrived at the scene to maintain order. The driver, Li Guodong, was temporarily detained at the Yixing County Public Security Bureau. The eight bodies were temporarily placed at Yixing Station for relatives to claim.

Changshu: Road Construction Workers Go on Hunger Strike to Demand Payment

A group of workers who were constructing the Changtai Highway in the Guli Village section had a conflict with the accountant over the settlement of accounts. With the help of the police, the workers were transported to Kunshan and dismissed. Now, more than 200 workers in the Baimao section have come to the city to stay in major hotels because the highway has been completed for many days and their wages have not been paid. The person in charge of the construction site, Tang Lianshi, suddenly disappeared. As a result, the workers were not given travel expenses, and their meals were also not secured. They then found Wang, the engineer of the Fuji Company, surrounded him, and demanded payment, but to no avail. The engineer and the workers did not eat all day. The head of the First District learned of this and telegraphed the Fuji Construction Site in Suzhou to send someone to Changshu to handle the matter and avoid accidents.

Change of County Trial Officer

The county trial officer of this county, Huang Jie, is now ordered to be transferred to Baoshan County to replace trial officer He Ruilin. Huang is quite tired of judicial affairs. After receiving the order, he went to the Suzhou High Court to request resignation. Now, trial officer He Ruilin of Baoshan County arrived in Changshu on the 6th of this month to take up his new post. He first went to the county government to pay his respects to County Magistrate Zhai and ask for instructions on everything. It is now known that He is from Jinhua County, Zhejiang Province, is 26 years old, graduated from Shanghai Law School, interned in Wujin for one year, and has served in judicial positions in Baoshan and other counties.

Haimen: Yang Zhaoti Case Investigated in Shanghai

Yang Zhaoti (also known as Little Yang) of Sanxing Town in the Second District was arrested and detained by the chief of the Seventh Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, Jing Bi, in the autumn of the 19th year of the Republic of China on suspicion of theft. He attempted to escape at night and was shot and killed by the police. The Sub-bureau reported it to the county government, which verified and collected the body. Later, Yu and others, believing that Chief Jing had fabricated false charges and committed intentional homicide, filed a complaint with the Supervisory Yuan with supporting evidence. After reviewing the case, the Supervisory Yuan sent the case to the Shanghai District Court for investigation. The District Court has set a hearing for the 10th of this month. Those summoned include the chief of the County Public Security Bureau Hao Zhiying, sub-bureau chief Jing Bi, and Yu and others.

Court Investigates Bribery Case Involving Party Headquarters

When this county implemented the public sale of opium, it established the Yuan Tai Company. It was agreed to bribe the county party headquarters and various agencies 340 yuan per month. Unexpectedly, someone submitted a photographic record of Yuan Tai Company's cash flow, and the Central Party Headquarters sent personnel to verify the facts. All members of the executive committee were dismissed and sent to the Shanghai District Court for trial. In addition to sentencing Cao Dingshi and others for fraud in the Three Factories case, the prosecutor also filed a public prosecution for the bribery case. It is said that the persons involved in this case include former executive committee members Huang Chengjiumao Dingyi and others. With the court date approaching, Huang Chengjiu and others took a boat from Niuhong Port to Shanghai yesterday to find a solution, but with the evidence being solid, it is feared that they will not escape the law.

Ningbo: Salt Police Accidentally Kill Villager While Suppressing Smuggling

In Tianyuanshi, Cui Chen Township, Fu Fang area of the Sixth District of Yuyao, there have recently been a large number of private salt smugglers smuggling private salt. The salt police team's patrol boat learned of this and sent a patrol boat to Cui Chen Township to investigate. At about 6:00 AM yesterday (the 5th), the team received a report that a large number of private salt smugglers would be passing through here. The salt police, armed with guns, ambushed in a remote location to wait. At that time, villagers Chen Zongshun and his son were going to Lishan Hospital for medical treatment and passed through the area. The salt police suspected them of being smugglers and immediately fired a warning shot. Unexpectedly, a bullet hit Chen Zongshun in the head, and he fell to the ground and died. The salt police fled in panic after realizing the accident. Afterwards, the deceased's son, Chen Zhangxian, filed a complaint with the Yuyao County Court, which sent personnel to investigate and handle the matter.

Soldiers and Bandits Clash, Hostage Escapes Dangerously

Xu Baodian, a resident of Chaijia in Tanhou Township, Yuyao, who is from a relatively well-off family. A few days ago, Xu received more than one hundred silver dollars, which aroused the covetousness of bandits. At more than 10:00 PM that night, six or seven bandits suddenly came, each armed with a wooden-cased gun, broke into the house. They then kidnapped Xu when they found no money. It was then learned of by the Tianyuan Town Regular Team. The team leader Xu Zhitang led his team to pursue them. When they arrived at Santangxia, they saw the bandits sitting on the ground. As the team was about to go forward to arrest them, the bandits opened fire to resist. The team members immediately returned fire. For a time, gunshots rang out incessantly, and bullets flew like rain. Soon, the bandits were unable to resist and fled in all directions. The kidnapped Xu Baodian was able to escape danger.

Special Article

Reducing Railway Freight Rates and Developing Rural Economies (4) Wu Shaozeng

(1) Production Aspects: The selling price of agricultural products in the consumer market is generally bound by the prevailing market price. Only those of particularly excellent quality can escape this. Therefore, its planned selling price must be close to the market price in order to participate in the competition; otherwise, it will be rejected or suffer losses. Freight is the factor that increases its cost and raises its selling price. Since freight becomes more expensive with distance, the transportation of agricultural products must reach a point where the freight is appropriate for its affordability. Beyond this, due to excessive costs and high selling prices, there is no way to gain a foothold in the consumer market, and progress will inevitably be hindered. For example, the annual production of cotton in Henan is about 16 million kilograms (according to statistics from the 22nd year of the Republic of China), but very little of it appears in markets such as Shanghai. Also, the annual production of rice in Sichuan is about 120 million shi, which is more than enough for self-sufficiency within Sichuan, but in markets such as Nanjing and Shanghai, which are farther away, there is very little Sichuan rice available. All of this is limited by transportation and freight rates (of course, not just railway freight rates), resulting in a state of oversupply within a short-range scope. As a result, the only option is to lower the price or reduce the total production. The cotton in Shaanxi is known as a famous variety, but the statistics for the 22nd year of the Republic of China show that it produced only 500,000 kilograms, which clearly demonstrates that the land was not fully utilized. For example, Shaanxi produced more than 21 million shi of wheat in the 20th year of the Republic of China, but it was reduced to more than 13.9 million shi in the 22nd year of the Republic of China. Although there are differences in the richness of the years, it cannot be denied that it is also due to the lack of full utilization of human resources. (To be continued)

Reading Q&A

The Problem of Women's Self-Study After Marriage (Continued 4)

Let's talk about the husband's role again. Women's self-study is inherently a personal issue for women, one that others cannot solve. However, because husbands are often the supporters of the family system and live with their wives, their every move has a great impact on women's self-study, and they bear considerable responsibility for solving the problem of women's self-study.

Like Mr. Liu's friend, introducing books to his wife is certainly necessary, and he should do his best to cater to her preferences (without relying on his own opinions) and buy more books and newspapers for her to browse, to gradually arouse her interest. However, this is not the most fundamental method, which is why Mr. Liu's friend still faced rejection from his wife. The most fundamental method is not to treat women as one's own captives, but to increase her courage to enter society and build the love between them on jointly striving for a career (including studying). Thus, on the one hand, it is necessary to reduce the contradictions between her life and thoughts, that is, to reduce her responsibilities for trivial family matters as much as possible, so that she has leisure to breathe. In this way, she will naturally reduce the depression of family life and the need to seek improper stimulation. (It is impossible to ask her to be a loyal housewife on the one hand and to work hard at studying on the other hand. This is merely an illusion arising from the husband's own contradictory old and new thoughts.) On the other hand, it is to increase her interest in self-study, which has already been discussed above.

In short, to say it again, the problem of women's self-study after marriage is related to the entire problem of women's liberation, and a satisfactory solution can only be obtained by striving for women's liberation.

Finally, the discussion in this article, based on Mr. Liu's letter, concerns general educated women, and does not specifically address the self-study of female workers and shop assistants, which is a major shortcoming. This shortcoming will only be filled when the opportunity arises.

Ministry of Education Explanation

The Problem of Vocational School Graduates Continuing Their Education

(Nanjing, 7th) The Ministry of Education issued an order to Tongji University on the 7th to explain the issue of vocational school graduates continuing their education, stating briefly that graduates of junior vocational schools may apply to senior vocational schools and high schools, but not to normal schools. Graduates of senior vocational schools may, in accordance with Article 3 of the regulations for universities and revised vocational schools, apply separately with the qualifications of graduates of equivalent schools.

Ministry of Education Explanation of Regulations for Studying Abroad

The Ministry of Education responded to the Hubei Provincial Government regarding the interpretation of Article 47 of the Hubei Provincial Regulations for Studying Abroad, stating briefly that it had received an inquiry regarding how Article 47 of the Provincial Regulations for Studying Abroad should be interpreted and supplemented, and requested a reply after review. It was found that according to the provisions of this article, if a publicly funded student simultaneously receives a Boxer Indemnity subsidy or other subsidy, the original provincial funding should be immediately stopped, and the provincial funding received from the date of receiving other subsidies should be recovered. The suspension of this funding is a form of sanction against publicly funded students who fail to comply with the regulations. A publicly funded student loses his or her publicly funded status after the funding is suspended. This loss of status cannot be restored even if the publicly funded student stops receiving other subsidies after being sanctioned. A corresponding response is hereby given for reference.

National Academic Work

Consultation Center to be Established Soon

The organizational regulations for the National Academic Work Consultation Center have been drafted by the Ministry of Education and sent to the National Economic Commission for approval. They will be announced simultaneously once the candidate for the director is finalized. Previously, the two departments had tentatively decided on a candidate who is currently the dean of a certain college in a national university in Shanghai and has other duties, but he has indicated that he will not accept the position. The departments need to find another candidate for the director, and they are currently in discussions. A decision is expected soon. The center will have investigation sections to investigate the status of academic staff in specialized schools and universities at home and abroad in order to introduce them to jobs. The original intention was to establish an overseas academic work consultation center in Geneva in addition to the domestic consultation center in order to conduct international investigations and liaisons. However, due to limited funding, the overseas center will not be established for the time being. The monthly cost of the domestic center alone is 3,000 yuan, most of which will be borne by the National Economic Commission, and the Ministry of Education will bear less than the Commission. The center will be established soon, and the organizational regulations will also be announced.

Hebei Education Department Admits Naval Students

(Tianjin, 7th) The Hebei Education Department has completed the examination for naval students recommended by the department and has announced the list of eight students admitted, including Yu Xin and Liu Zengqian. They gathered at the Education Department at 2 p.m. on the 6th to receive training and are scheduled to go to Beijing on the 20th to enroll in school.

Medical Education Committee Continued Meeting Yesterday

(Nanjing, 7th) The Ministry of Education's Medical Education Committee continued its third meeting at 8:30 a.m. on the 7th. The same number of people attended as on the 6th. Chairman Yan Fuqing adjourned the meeting at noon with the following resolutions: (1) Approved the curriculum outline for medical vocational schools; (2) Elected Weng Zhilong, Wu Xiangfeng, and Yan Fuqing as members of the drafting committee for the preparatory standards for medical colleges and medical vocational schools, to be convened by Weng.

Municipal Education Bureau to Issue Certificates on Schedule

Certificates for Summer School and Summer Lecture Attendees

The Municipal Education Bureau issued a special announcement, Education No. 23180, yesterday regarding the scheduled issuance of certificates to qualified students of the summer school and summer lectures held this year. The announcement stated that the fourth summer school and the second summer lecture series for teachers of private registered primary schools organized by the bureau this year have ended, and the grades for each subject have been reviewed. The list of qualified students will be published in the bureau's Education Weekly. Certificates of qualification will be issued to the students at the bureau's office during office hours from September 12th to 15th. All summer school students, including Yang Ding and 253 others, and summer lecture students, including Huang Hao and 158 others, should come to the Third Section of the bureau to collect their certificates on time and without delay. This announcement is made to ensure that everyone is informed.

Student Union Pursues Legal Action

Huang Kewu Leads Meeting to Decide on Multiple Important Matters

Lawyer Li Qian Hired to Pursue Legal Action; Formal Lawsuit Filed

(Shenshi News) Since Shi Yunjin (24 years old, from Haimen), the principal of Dajiang Vocational School on Tangshan Road, colluded with his father, Tang Min, and his brothers, Yuncheng and Yunlong, to embezzle funds and absconded, all the students of the school have lost their homes. Every day, dozens of students gather in front of the school to hold meetings to discuss the aftermath and how to deal with the situation. It has recently been learned that the school's student union has resolved to hire lawyer Li Qian to file a lawsuit with the court, requesting legal action. A reporter from Shenshi News met with the person in charge of the union at his residence yesterday. According to him, all 150 students of the school were extremely indignant after learning that Principal Shi Yunjin and others had colluded to embezzle funds and absconded. They immediately convened an emergency meeting of all students to discuss the following measures: (1) Due to the lack of experience and ability of the students, former teacher Huang Kewu and others were specially invited to lead the handling of all follow-up matters (passed); (2) Lawyer Li Qian was hired as a legal advisor to handle all litigation and non-litigation matters of the union (passed); (3) Yu Yan, Hu Bin, Long Yunmin, Chen Zhifan, Zhang Beiying, Yu Zhimei, and six others were elected as representatives, led by Mr. Huang Kewu, to handle all external affairs (passed); (4) A petition was submitted to the Education Bureau in the name of all students (approved); (5) Yu Yan, Wang Changxun, Chen Liezhong, Zhou Chenggen, and Gong Yunmin were elected as executive committee members (passed). It is reported that the union will issue a declaration to attract attention and assistance from all walks of life. On the other hand, lawyer Li Qian has filed a lawsuit with the criminal division of the Shanghai First Special District Court, and the trial is expected to be held soon.

Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation

Experimental Research Conference to be Held Tomorrow

Starting at 9 a.m. at the Provincial Shanghai Experimental Primary School

Approximately 20 Member Schools Participating

The Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation Experimental Research Conference will be held at the Shanghai Experimental Primary School of Jiangsu Province on Shangwen Road in this city, starting at 9 a.m. on the 9th of this month, to discuss the work plans for experimental research in various schools. Details are as follows:

Participating Schools: The schools that should participate in the conference include Shanghai Experimental Primary School, Nanjing Experimental Primary School, Suzhou Experimental Primary School, Zhenjiang Experimental Primary School, Yangzhou Experimental Primary School, Xuzhou Primary School, Nantong Primary School, Songjiang Primary School, Zhenjiang Affiliated Primary School, Xishi Affiliated Primary School, Rush Affiliated Primary School, Su Female Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Tai Shi Affiliated Primary School, Huai Shi Affiliated Primary School, Hai Shi Affiliated Primary School, Xu Female Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Qixia Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Wujiang Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Huangdu Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Luoshe Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, Guanyun Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, and Xingfu Rural Normal School Affiliated Primary School, totaling more than 20 schools. Each school will send its director of experimental research or research director to attend.

Draft Regulations: The draft regulations of the conference are as follows: Article 1: The conference is subordinate to the Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation. Article 2: The purpose of the conference is to coordinate the division of labor and cooperation in the experimental research activities of all schools in the federation. Article 3: The conference shall be organized by five schools elected by the Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation at its general meeting. Two schools shall be re-elected each year, and the schools withdrawing shall be determined by lot. Article 4: The conference shall mutually elect one school as the executive school. Article 5: The conference shall convene once per semester, convened by the executive school. The federation's schools' personnel in charge of experimental research and promotion must also be notified to attend and participate in the discussions during the meeting. Article 6: The duties of the conference are as follows: (1) To carry out the experimental research work assigned by the general meeting; (2) To investigate and organize the plans and results of experimental research in various schools; (3) To discuss all issues raised by various schools regarding the progress of experimental research work. Article 7: The conference may contact relevant domestic academic organizations to jointly conduct experimental research work. Article 8: The conference may hire experts to guide all ongoing work. Article 9: The expenses of the conference shall be provided by the Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation. Article 10: These regulations must be reviewed and approved by the council of the federation. Article 11: These regulations may be amended at any time if they are not perfect and submitted to the council of the federation for review.

Methods of Implementation: The methods of implementation for the experimental research of each school in 1934 will be discussed at the meeting. The outline of the plan formulated by the Shanghai Experimental Primary School of Jiangsu Province is as follows: (A) Regarding Experimentation: (1) Experimentation with Patriotic Education Programs: (a) Vigorously implement physical training, (b) Vigorously implement group training, (c) Vigorously implement production training, (2) Experimentation with New Educational Methods: (a) Continue to experiment with the whole teaching method in lower grades, (b) Continue to experiment with the problem teaching method in middle grades, (c) Continue to experiment with individual teaching method in senior grades, (3) Comparative Experimentation of Teaching Problems: (a) Experimental problems, (b) Experimental plan, (B) Regarding Research: (1) Subject Research: (a) Civics training, (b) Hygiene, physical education and music, (c) Chinese language, (d) Arithmetic, (e) Social and natural science, (f) Manual arts, (2) Special Topic Research

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Copper Oxide Detection

— Shi Huayu

Usually, the detection work of a radio is performed by a vacuum tube, but now it has been discovered that copper oxide (CuO) can be used as a high-frequency rectifier, and the experimental results are also satisfactory. When a high-frequency voltage above ten volts is input, the detection efficiency of copper oxide is very good. Even when the amplitude modulation component is 70%, the low-frequency voltage output after its detection is the same as the magnitude of the input high-frequency voltage, with no loss. And after intensive measurement, although the high-frequency voltage input is higher, the detection completed by copper oxide is still linear. Therefore, the distortion on the curved part of the characteristic curve caused by using ordinary vacuum tubes as detectors can be avoided. And considering the aspect of saving the radio's space, copper oxide is also better than vacuum tubes. Because copper oxide can be much smaller in diameter than vacuum tubes with the same efficiency. At the same time, we can use four pieces of copper oxide for full-wave rectification or full-wave detection (DoppelwegGieichrichtung). The area of four pieces of copper oxide put together is only as large as the space for a lamp holder.

At the same time, copper oxide is much easier to manufacture than vacuum tubes, and the value is much lower than vacuum tubes, and the efficiency is so high. It is likely that it will take the detection position of vacuum tubes in the near future. As for the high-frequency voltage above ten volts, we can easily obtain it by using one or two stages of high-frequency amplification. Copper oxide also has a most important characteristic, which is the convenience of fading compensation (FADINGKOMPENSATION), because we only need to adjust its detection performance under a high-frequency voltage of ten to one hundred volts.

As for what should be paid the most attention to during assembly, it is necessary to maximize the current passing through it. The most appropriate coupling between the copper oxide detector and the high-frequency amplifier can be found in the attached diagram. In order to make it clear to the reader, the fading compensation section is also drawn in the figure, so the copper oxide in the figure is not completely used for detection. One of them is used to manage the miss-out compensation and is transmitted to the gate of the variable amplification coefficient amplifier tube at high frequency and intermediate frequency, and adjust the input signal voltage.

At the same time, because its output voltage after detection is extremely high (the low-frequency voltage output at 70% amplitude modulation is almost the same as the input high-frequency voltage, and the noise component (klirrfoktorR) is less than 0.5%), it is not difficult to directly excite the final vacuum tube. Resistor B in the figure can be used for volume adjustment.

After using a high-frequency copper oxide rectifier, the radio's installation can be greatly simplified. Therefore, ordinary applications use multi-grid tubes, such as variable amplification coefficient pentodes—the characteristics that input power can be very small—for high amplification. Low amplification and superheterodyne local oscillators are handled by ordinary triodes. Readers, imagine if there is a radio whose high amplification uses a variable amplification coefficient pentode, the detection uses copper oxide for full-wave rectification, the low amplification uses a triode final stage power amplifier tube, and there is also a copper oxide fading compensation section. In fact, this effect is better than the wireless machine used by the three-tube radio, but it only uses two vacuum tubes, and one of them is a very cheap final stage power amplifier tube. Such a radio can be considered popularized!

How to Add and Adjust a Tuning Meter

— Ming Xiang

Many radios, although they have the function of automatic volume control, do not have a tuning meter installed. When adjusting the radio station, the most sensitive point cannot be observed with the naked eye, which is a pity. If you want to make your radio more noble, you can follow the description in this article. You only need to add a common milliampere meter to achieve the goal.

The first step is to study the circuit of your radio to determine where the meter should be connected. Usually, the most superior position is the vacuum tube in the high-frequency or intermediate-frequency stage that is automatically controlled. Its screen circuit is connected to the positive pole of the B voltage after the filter. If more than one stage is controlled, you can choose any one. As shown in the figure, at points A and B, if the control voltages received by each vacuum tube are not the same, it is best to connect to the largest stage. In this way, the meter pointer will move more dramatically, and the adjustment will be more obvious. The meter must be connected to the B+ end of the filter, otherwise, the high-frequency current will pass through the meter, making the amplification stage unstable and damaging the meter.

For convenience, the meter can also be connected to the common lead connecting B+ of each controlled tube. In this way, the current passing through is increased, and the rate of change is still the same as before, as shown in point C in the figure. But be careful not to accidentally connect the meter to the common lead of other vacuum tubes that are not automatically volume controlled. The common lead of each controlled tube, if the control voltage of each tube is different, the indicator meter cannot be connected. Pay attention to this point.

The range of the meter should be smaller than the current value in the circuit where it is connected when there is no signal input. Assuming that the current in this circuit is IO M·A·, the range of the meter cannot exceed .5 Ma', such as o-I or o-2M·a·. Because in this way, the pointer of the meter can be calibrated to the maximum degree when the radio is not adjusted to the radio station. Later, if there is a signal input, the distance the pointer jumps is the largest, and the function of the indicator meter is the most sensitive. The calibration method is to connect a variable resistor across the meter as a shunt. Change the resistance of this shunt so that the pointer of the meter shows the maximum degree when there is no signal input.

This kind of indicator meter is extremely sensitive. Even if an extremely weak signal cannot be detected by an ordinary shadow-type indicator meter, the pointer of this meter can still move significantly. Another advantage is that even if the radio is disturbed by atmospheric electricity, the meter pointer will not tremble too much, so that it is impossible to distinguish the signals of weak radio stations.

Using a Voltmeter as an Ammeter

— Yong Yan

An ammeter connected in series with a resistor with a very large ohmic value becomes a voltmeter. Because according to "Ohm's Law", the current passing through this ammeter is proportional to the voltage connected to the two ends of this ammeter: therefore, it is only necessary to change the scale to the corresponding number of volts, and it can be used to measure voltage. From this, we can know that a voltmeter can be used as an ammeter if a way can be found. Now, the method of modification is described as follows:

A. Disassemble the voltmeter and remove the series resistor to make an ammeter. (If the resistor is connected, it is still a voltmeter) At this point, the scale of the meter can be calibrated with another accurate ammeter. If the range that this ammeter can measure is still too small, a resistor can be connected in parallel as a shunt to increase its range. The calculation method of this resistor is R = r ÷ (N-I), where R is the ohmic value of the shunt, R is the internal resistance of the ammeter, and N is the multiple to be increased. For example, there is an ammeter with an internal resistance of one ohm and a measurable range of 0.1 amps. If you want to make it measurable up to half an amp, how many ohms of resistor should be connected in parallel? In this case, r is one and N is five: substituting into the above formula, we get R is 0.25 ohms, so we know that a 0.25 ohm resistor should be connected in parallel.

B. The series resistor of the low-voltage section of an ordinary voltmeter is only two to three hundred ohms, so it can also be used to measure current. (Please refer to Mr. Kejun's manuscript in issue 32 of this publication) The conversion of its reading can be done using Ohm's Law. For example, there is a voltmeter with a low-voltage section of ten volts and an internal resistance (see note) of 400 ohms; then when the pointer points to ten volts, the current passing through this meter is ten out of four hundredths of an amp, that is, twenty-five milliamps; therefore, the first volt on the original meter corresponds to two and a half milliamps. This ammeter can also be connected to a shunt as in method A to increase the range of measurable current.

Among the above two methods, method A is more accurate, while method B is only limited to measuring the current in circuits with high resistance, otherwise the measured number is unreliable. When using method B, if the resistance in the measured circuit and the internal resistance of the meter are known, the measured number can be corrected. The method is as follows:

First, use the meter to measure the current amount I, and then use the following formula to find the accurate current amount I = (iR + ir) ÷ R, where r is the internal resistance of the meter, and R is the resistance in the circuit other than the meter.

(Note) The internal resistance of the voltmeter is mostly marked on the meter or in the instruction manual. If not, it can be measured with an ohmmeter or Wheatstone bridge; or it can be calculated using the following method. The method is to connect a resistor R in series with the voltmeter, and connect its two ends to a battery with a voltage of E; if the pointer of the meter points to e volts, then the internal resistance r of the meter is r = e × R ÷ (E - e). According to this method, calculate several rs with different values of R and E, and then find their average value as the accurate value of the internal resistance of the voltmeter.

Single-Tube Radio Circuit with 58 as Detector

— Zi Pei

When using a triode to make a single-tube machine, it is always considered that the volume is too low to satisfy the desire. Amateur home users often change multi-pole new vacuum tubes into single-tube machines, and the results are often unexpected. The filament current is supplied by a modified ordinary electric bell square shed, the voltage is 2.5 volts, and the current is one amp. As a result, prices for each month only rose by 0.05 to 0.1 or 0.2 cents. In the afternoon, the weather cleared up, and there was some discussion that this year's climate was dry, and new cotton developed earlier. Farmers in various villages had already harvested 50% of the crop. The second and third sessions trended downward. As a result, prices for each month fell by 0.05 to 0.1 cents.
