Yingkou Gang Actively Handles Term Flour

Yesterday's flour market saw an initial flatness followed by stability in each month. The quoted prices of foreign wheat in Chicago and Canada both improved by about 0.1 or 0.2 dollars. When opening prices were quoted, the market situation for this month was still flat, but when opening prices for October were quoted, the manufacturers slightly slacked off on selling, and the minds of those outside the industry turned lively. Furthermore, because the Yingkou Gang had a small amount of business, each month turned slightly profitable in the midst of calmness. By the time the afternoon market opened, transactions were relatively quiet, and the buying and selling of each month was only more than 200,000 bags. However, because factory output was not abundant and those floating in the air outside the industry did not continue to sell, the market atmosphere became slightly better. As a result, this month rose by 0.02 dollars compared to the previous day, October rose by 0.035 dollars, November rose by 0.025 dollars, December rose by 0.0175 dollars, January improved by 0.0225 dollars, and February rose by 0.025 dollars.

Figure One, Figure Two

LL1L2 are ordinary three-circuit coils, adjusted with a variable capacitor Cr (also adjustable with a push-pull frame). C and C1 are .○○○35 variable capacitors, C2 is .○○○25 fixed capacitor, R is 2 to 4 megaohms, R·F·C· is a high-frequency choke for broadcasting. OGS connects to the highest voltage of the B battery, which is adjusted by a 6,000-ohm variable resistor R1. This can improve the old sound quality and volume to the best level. If a resistor adjustment is not used, it can be connected to the B battery at 90 volts or 135 volts. In short, the voltage of GS greatly affects the volume and sound quality of this machine. If the voltage is too high, the sound will be suppressed, and if it is too low, the sound will be light and the quality poor.

The soldering of 58 is shown in Figure 2. The cathode grid Sn and the cathode C are connected. The cap is the control grid, and the screen grid is connected to a 6,000-ohm volume adjuster. The cathode is connected to B negative. The rest is connected as a triode, except for the filament H, which cannot be connected to the B battery because it uses alternating current.

The antenna circuit of this machine has at most twelve turns. Too many turns will result in poor selectivity. I have used an indoor antenna in Wusong to listen to various large and small radio stations in Shanghai and Nanjing. Sound can be played in the loudspeaker day and night. If an outdoor antenna is used, the results should be even better.

This machine can be converted to full AC operation. Rectifiers such as 82'80 can be used. Comrades who like to assemble and disassemble may wish to try it.

Small Experience

### Substitutes for Solder

— Shan Zhang

Many people think that cigarette wrappers are made of tin foil, but the ones currently used are all made of lead foil, so soldering them is unsuccessful because aluminum, when heated, turns into aluminum oxide, a non-conductive material.

If we want to find a substitute, we can only use toothpaste tubes. Toothpaste tubes are indeed made of tin. When using them, remove the outer lacquer with sandpaper, and then it can be used. If the lacquer is not removed, soldering will be difficult because the organic matter will carbonize. In addition, the outer shell of soft film packaging can also be used. It is not necessary to sand it, which seems convenient, but it is not as easy to find as a toothpaste tube.

It is very expensive to buy a small amount of solder from a coppersmith, and it is not worthwhile to buy a lot, so using our method is very good.

### Self-Made Rotary Filament Switch

— Chuan Xun

A. Bakelite Board B. Copper Pieces (2) C. Key Turn D. Complete

The filament switch is an indispensable component on a radio. There are many types, and their structure is very complicated. It is not easy for us to make it ourselves without adequate machinery, because when the circuit is open, all conductors must be tightly connected without loosening in order to reduce the resistance in the circuit. When the circuit is closed, the insulation must be good and firm to prevent the possibility of current leakage. Also, there must be elastic assistance when switching. Inexpensive ones are always impractical, so when choosing a switch, in addition to meeting the above conditions, we must also consider its price and the space it occupies. The following is a simple and practical switch-making method suitable for us to make ourselves.

A is the style of the bakelite or hard rubber board required. The three holes can be hot drilled.

B is the style of the elastic copper piece, two pieces in total.

C is a hardwood turning key. Half is a cylinder, and half is a larger square column, with thick copper wire wrapped around it.

Then insert the round rod of the turning key into the large hole in the bakelite. Then press the two copper pieces tightly on both sides (see Figure D, each fixed with screws at the bottom).

It is best to add a spiral tube where the round rod is inserted for mounting on the radio.

Internal and External News

Opening of the Mainland Telecommunications Engineering Training Institute: The Mainland Telecommunications Engineering Training Institute, located at 319 Nanjing Road, Shanghai, opened its autumn semester on September 5th and is scheduled to begin classes on the 15th. It is reported that the school's wireless telegraphy and amateur telecommunications refresher courses still have a few openings. If they are not filled before the start of classes, students can still register for admission. It is also reported that in order to assist poor students in studying wireless electricity, the school has added ten half-fee students to the refresher course. Those who are interested in enrolling and whose families are indeed in difficulty can apply for half-fee admission before the 12th. In addition, the school's correspondence school offers wireless engineering and wired telephone courses. In addition to the usual free wireless electricity textbooks, enrolled students will also receive fifteen scholarships in the form of radios, which will be awarded to graduates with excellent grades.

Wireless Electricity Department of the Third China Refresher School: The Third China Vocational Refresher School on Lujiabang Road, Xiaoximen, has a wireless electricity department. The teachers hired, such as engineer Cao from Dahua Wireless Electricity Company and Mr. Wang from the International Wireless Electricity Station, are all knowledgeable and experienced and extremely enthusiastic in teaching. The tuition fee is also very low. It can not only train professional and technical personnel but also provide amateurs with the opportunity to learn and discuss. It is reported that this semester, teachers and students will cooperate to build a shortwave broadcasting machine for research and experimentation with shortwave wireless electricity. The school is scheduled to open on September 10th. Recently, there has been a continuous stream of people requesting prospectuses and registering.

Autumn Ode

— Lü Qian

Autumn is great, it is lovely! Autumn is indeed the best season of the year. It does not have the cold and sternness of winter, nor the sultry heat of summer; it is even more lively and refined than the annoying spring! It can indeed bring a quiet sense of pleasure and comfort to people from a desolate soul!

Autumn has descended on the world in this way! These green mountains and this green water, how beautiful! How bright! The changing autumn clouds and the continuous autumn rain, how well they can express the poetry of autumn! In the bustling city, autumn shows a proud and composed beauty, revealing the new autumn season of "curtains rolled up by the golden wind, garden condensed with jade dew." Following this, the modern girls with graceful waists and hair in elegant sideburns have changed into new autumn fashions with narrow sleeves and long robes. Facing the soft and refreshing breeze, they brush open the sleeves on both sides, revealing their elastic thighs and silver high-heeled shoes. As their delicate feet move rhythmically, they emit a shining silver light. Their shallow dimples often emerge from their small cherry lips, revealing the comfort and joy that autumn bestows on their hearts! All the people seem to have been suffocated by the scorching heat and only by the help of autumn can they exhale a breath of dirty air and be as active as before! People express infinite goodwill towards the arrival of autumn. In such an environment, autumn is sufficient to console and pride itself!

In the countryside, autumn shows a more charming and natural beauty. Countless fields of half-green and half-yellow rice ears have grown very plump. Each grain of white rice is wrapped in a thin husk, both tender and substantial, swaying in the wind, waiting for the hardworking farmers to harvest them in the near future. At this time, the old farmers wearing bamboo hats smile broadly. One can imagine! They deeply feel the benefits that autumn bestows on them, containing infinite joy!

How autumn makes me miss and yearn! I wish the beautiful and serene autumn would reside in the world forever!

Anti-Lament for Autumn

— Mei Xue

An old gentleman, known for his poetry, is once again raising his shoulders and chanting. Seeing the phoenix leaves dancing in the air, he cries in a mournful tone and chants a poem lamenting autumn. A young boy, out of curiosity, hastily asks: "Old man, you are asking for redress, your lament for autumn is unwarranted!" The old gentleman angrily says: "You young fellow, do not speak much. "Alas, the atmosphere of autumn," is the sigh of Senior Official Song. "I only hear the chirping of insects on all four walls, as if to aid my sigh," is the lament of Ouyang Zi. The ancients were still like that, let alone us? You young fellow, do not speak much."

After this statement, the young boy's chatterbox opened up: "Old gentleman, you are mistaken! Autumn is the golden age of harvest, autumn is the beautiful period of results. There is only joy, no sadness. The old-fashioned poet who groans without illness, sees the yellow leaves falling one by one, as if the trees have been wounded. Once they fall, they become withered beyond recognition. Who knew that it was a huge misunderstanding? Without fallen leaves, there would be no results. If every plant and tree all preserved their colorful state, if the flowers did not wither and the leaves did not fall, then how could there be a beautiful harvest? Without a harvest, then the fields would not produce grains, and the forests would not yield fruits, wouldn't that cause a huge panic in society? It can be seen that the season of autumn is giving us a very hopeful period. Autumn has arrived, everything is ripe, grains will soon be on the threshing floor, fruits will soon be on the market. What old farmers and gardeners are eagerly awaiting is this autumn season. Poets should resonate with the masses. When they are moved to poetry, they should say things that welcome autumn and look forward to its arrival. "The autumn wind rises, the leaves fall," these are auspicious omens. They should not groan without illness and make depressing poems. They should not parrot others. Senior Official Song sighed, and you also want to sigh. Ouyang Zi lamented, and you also want to lament. Have you become an echo of Senior Official Song and Ouyang Zi? Poets must have an independent nature. It is already unacceptable to pick up the spit of the ancients, let alone become an echo of the ancients? Old gentleman, you are mistaken!"

Once the chatterbox was opened, the old gentleman had already disappeared. Since he is not chanting poetry, let the young boy babble a few words:

People say, the autumn wind shakes the hundred grasses, I say: the autumn wind becomes ten thousand treasures. "The waves of Dongting, the leaves fly," this is an omen of having autumn. A foolish poet composes lament for autumn, it is said: "what the wicked love."

Two Views of Autumn

— Liang Xiaohong

The countryside is a tea-green color, with the leaves of old maple trees dotted here and there like vermilion lips. A thin purple haze floats in the atmosphere. The calm surface of the river slowly sends autumn waves to people. In the warm grassland at sunset, there is a feeling of tenderness and attachment. In the evening, the clear and bright moonlight is sprinkled in the space. In the broken bricks and grass, autumn insects are playing a symphony.... Ah, lovely autumn, it is indeed the most moving season of the year! It is like a young woman in the style of Lin Daiyu, with a simple and dignified appearance, a silent and reserved personality. In its beauty, it carries an inviolable solemnity. In its tranquility, it contains sincere and ardent emotions. Everything about it has the charm of making people pity and love it. In its embrace, we simply don't feel uncomfortable anymore!

However, on the other hand, it is scary enough, with everywhere lurking the opportunity for desolation and killing. Bellicose crickets are one of its products. People, inadvertently, at any time have the possibility of being attacked and killed by disease. Epidemic diseases such as dysentery and vomiting are its most terrifying demonstrations. Don't you hear? The clinics of epidemic doctors have more than two hundred patients every day! Ah, murderous autumn, it is a difficult hurdle that people must pass through every year. We must all be careful not to be swallowed by it!

Autumn, is autumn ultimately lovely or terrible?

Reproductive Capacity of Autumn Flies

— Qing Qu

"Flies, a single thing, speaking of it, is truly so formidable! Yet in our ancient books, it was thought that "blue flies disorder color, houseflies disorder sound," like the line in the Book of Songs, Minor Odes of the Kingdom, Crow with Young, "buzzing blue flies." The commentary says, "Flies as insects, pollute white making it black, pollute black making it white," which is only a metaphor for petty people, reversing good and evil; until the Biography of Wei Xiao in the Later Han Dynasty, there was "The flight of a housefly, no more than a few steps, relies on the tail of a fine steed, and can sever its group," only then did one know the ability of "flies" is really very great, if it relies on the veins of side power, is this not a very terrible culprit?

This year, in the summertime, good! Heaven, like a fire, emits blazing sunshine, shines on the ground, so that the rivers dry and the water is shallow, even the paddy fields that are planted with rice will dry and crack, making the green seedlings wilt and die; so the many other kinds of pests are affected quite a lot, difficult to breed, exterminating a large amount of molecules, then: speaking fairly, in terms of farming, it is inevitable that there will be a poor harvest, becoming a barren appearance, and in terms of human health, because the weather is dry, the air is dry and hot, all kinds of microorganisms, etc.; there is no place to attach themselves to survive, on the contrary, they have gained a lot of benefits, but ordinary people who lack common sense are unaware!

Now! It has already entered autumn, everyone thinks that the sultry heat can recede and the new coolness attacks people, is it not like the dog days that make people want to drink to death! Oh! Who knows that the weather is still very hot, and like "flies" that are a great enemy to our lives, have become prosperous with a buzzing sound; what is the reason for this?

I dare not speak recklessly, in reality autumn is more unclean than summer, in reality, there are many, just looking at the streets, watermelon rinds, bean pod rinds, corn cobs, everywhere are enough to attract countless "flies" to gather, in this way: "flies" naturally gather more and more every day; according to scientists, "flies" from eggs to larvae, to the adult stage, although there are differences in length, every time they lay eggs, hey! At least there must be one hundred and dozens, calculated with half male and half female, from then on, constantly mating, their children and grandchildren, about ten generations, then: the lineage of "flies", does it not occupy a hundred trillion trillion times how much? Yo! This alarming great enemy of life, must be in the hot weather of autumn, think of ways to eliminate it!

Postscript

I and the cuckoo among birds are the same sorrowful seeds between heaven and earth, so even in spring and summer, worrying about the country and the family, I often have a lament for autumn. Now it is autumn again! This "autumn rain, autumn wind, sorrowful grain people" autumn, my sorrow is needless to say. On a boring autumn night, I examined the manuscripts from writers from all directions, and there were many writings about "autumn," so I made a special issue of "autumn" to show solidarity. This is the postscript. In the autumn of Jiaxu, Zhou Shoujuan wrote at the Violet Hermitage.

Autumn Insect Chat

— Huo Xueming

As usual, I should write a small introduction here, the best thing is: "A year is easy, it is autumn wind again." In the autumn wind, dark crickets are chirping, the sound is so powerful that people feel a kind of interest. If you lived in the countryside in your childhood, you must have listened intently under the eaves of your house, beside the flower beds in the yard, with your ears pricked up. Your heart was laughing, but you were calm. Once you determined the source of the sound, you would sneak over, hold a golden thread cover, squat down, and quietly brighten your eyes. While gently moving the eaves, you would quickly cover the cricket with the golden thread cover. If it jumped and escaped, you would inevitably jump up and chase it. At this time, the courage of the chase was indeed very laughable.

However, catching crickets in childhood, like catching fireflies, was without purpose, only feeling it was fun. Later, seeing adults in tea houses using crickets, weighing them against each other, and using small grasses to provoke them to fight, thus determining that the owner who raised crickets would use money to determine the outcome; then one knew that crickets had another use, no wonder opium addicts went out all day to overturn bricks and pick tiles, even searching in tombs, in order to earn money.

But the parents at home, for children who did not study and write well, but caught crickets with wild children, the parents would definitely scold them for being unfilial, and would definitely not allow them to bring crickets home. Even if they secretly put the little insects in a matchbox (because they had no money and did not dare to buy a cricket pot openly), and put them on the corner of their pillow before going to bed, they could not help but cry out. As soon as the cry started, the parents would throw the matchbox into the spittoon, and say that people who catch crickets would become good-for-nothing hooligans like Wairentuzi, and Wairentuzi's shorts were indeed torn, only squatting beside the tomb all day with his ears pricked up.

One can imagine the wounds etched on the innocent heart of a child whose beloved chirping insect was thrown away. He was almost as sad as if he had lost his rocking horse or doll. However, he dared not rebel against his parents, he only hated his parents. Why were his parents not like A'Hu in the tea house treating their children! During the day, when Little Tiger caught a big cricket, his father stroked his hair, praised him repeatedly for being clever, and even scratched his thumb, looked at the cricket, and shouted loudly to people: "This is a general! Is this not a general! How loud it cries! How big its teeth are!"

It was enough not to praise him. But why can other people's children catch crickets, but his own cannot? If he cannot catch them, it is enough, why do you not let the ones that have already been caught go to the courtyard and let them live, but instead throw them into the spittoon to drown? You hear, after throwing them down, they keep crying, probably their wings are soaked in water, and also the sound of the matchbox hitting the copper spittoon, the cricket must be struggling, mourning, but.... Now half a point of sound has already disappeared, the night is so desolate, the child's heart is crying in the dark.

The above description, although it is my personal imagination, but the same facts will definitely exist. The feeling of resentment towards their parents at that time could not be avoided by anyone. When I was young, I was also very naughty. After being reprimanded by my mother for catching crickets once, I never dared to repeat the offense. However, at that time, I did not feel how bad it was to play with crickets. Of course, I did not understand that this kind of game would lose the will to be enterprising and indulge in the vulgar habit of gambling!

Later, after reading the History of the Song Dynasty, I felt that Jia Sidao, in the Banxian Hall, in addition to indulging in pleasure with concubines, actually neglected politics because he was obsessed with playing with crickets, and then I knew the reasons why my parents used to reprimand me. Shen Zhou passed Geling, and there was a poem about this incident saying:

"In the idle hall, the treasure pavilion is in the picture, heaven begged the lakes and mountains to support the prime minister. It is exactly the day of many events in Xiangfan, but he specializes in battle tests of autumn insects! ——Truly ironic and humorous! Little did he know that there were still juggling and shuttlecock kicking tricks that echoed before and after! As for what is said in the Legacy Matters of the Tianbao Era: "Every time autumn arrives, the concubines in the palace compete to catch crickets in small golden cages and place them beside their pillows to listen to their voices." This is similar to the meaning of the child secretly hiding crickets described above. However, at the same time, it can also be seen that the palace people of the dynasty have the sorrow of "not being able to see them for thirty-six years." Therefore, all poems that chant crickets mostly contain a desolating tone, such as Bai Juyi's "dark cricket chirping night is continuous," Zhang Lai's "the dark cricket in the stone bottom chirps at night first," Wen Tingyun's "the dry pond connects to the broken bank, the cold cricket chirps;" can make oneself seem to be between sand traces, in the quiet of the night, hearing the desolate chirping. I only wonder how those soldiers who are good at internal strife, killing each other, actually forget that the imperialists who are watching from the sidelines are using crickets to incite them, to provoke them to slaughter, and to observe the success or failure from the outside; what are their thoughts?

Strolling Alone on an Autumn Night

— Chen Liang

The night with the eyes of a lover so tender, is an autumn night! Lonely, lonely.

Carrying a collection of poems, I stepped out of Huage Gate, walking slowly on the green stone of the alley. Autumn insects were hiding in the holes at the foot of the wall, in the cracks of the stones, and in the piles of broken bricks, crying with sorrow, crying with bitterness, crying with the loneliness of the night.

The electric light of fifteen candlepower shone on this long alley, and the places not illuminated were darkly unfolding the wings of bats, filled with the autumnal night wind, blowing towards me, filling my chest, feeling the taste of desolation. Half of my thin, long shadow was attached to the white powder wall, and half of it was falling to the ground. People were sandwiched in the middle layer between the high walls, like a tame deer walking under the cliffs. Passing leisurely days.

Passing a bland, empty life, this desolate journey.

Walking out of the alley, Penglai Road, in the circle of the autumn moon, was lightly draped with a veil of poetry. The phoenix trees on the sidewalk were sighing, the autumn wind gave them the tone of sadness, the autumn moon reflected their weak shadows, the yellow leaves could not bear the destruction of the season, falling branch by branch, wandering everywhere, being trampled on by various different feet, people who had lost their souls, the decadent people in a declining life.

The door of "Qingjie Hall" was black and oily, the moonlight was blocked by the high fire wall, it seemed that many ghosts were holding a night dance party, hanging a trembling heart, constricting sweat pores, quickly passing by, the grass under the wall was sobbing in the autumn night wind.

Some low houses, some fences, some lights shining out from the cracks in the board doors. It was getting cold, there were no people camping out, leaving the door crowded with bottomless desolation, silence, and desolation. Like a lonely traveler on a deserted island, like a Mongolian nomad in the wilderness.

I ran into "Wenmiao Park," and the protein-colored lights were spying on the outline of the Eastern architecture. The moon was drunk in the creek, I opened the collection of poems and recited silently, and recited aloud the sentences that were enchanting, walking back and forth along the path covered with moonlight, the autumn night walker closed his eyes, and was a little drunk!

We Must Cry Out Against This Injustice

— Beast

—Regarding "Where Are the Great Works?"

Concerning the production of great works, I remember that as early as several months ago, Mr. Chen Boqi already discussed it in his article "The Requirements for Great Works." Afterward, in a certain monthly magazine, there was also a solicitation of essays on "Why Are There No Great Works Being Produced in China Currently," which many writers answered. Moreover, such discussions scattered in various places are even more numerous. In summary, they can be roughly divided into the following reasons:

1. Unfavorable environment.

2. Writers' abilities are insufficient, lacking courage.

3. The Monroe Doctrine of the literary world.

4. Chinese society is changing too rapidly, and the literary movement cannot keep up.

In fact, it is very difficult to objectively determine whether a work is great or not. What kind of work? What standards should be used to judge whether a work is great or not? In my opinion, if a writer can grasp the current real society and thoroughly base their work on new concepts, using realistic techniques to imply the trends of the times, they can become active in front of readers and become a great work. In other words, as long as it depicts reality truthfully, it can become a great work; as long as it truthfully depicts reality, it can become a historical monument.

From this, we can see that Mr. Hunren's eloquent discussion in the "Free Talk" section of the Shen Bao (30th) is inaccurate. Mr. Hunren said that the reason why great works are buried in wastepaper baskets is due to "the Monroe Doctrine of editors and the profit-seeking of bookstore owners, but the main responsibility should be assigned to the readers." I don't understand how Mr. Hunren slurred his words and dragged us readers into this. It is truly a sin that only Heaven knows. Such a major sin that damages the entire Chinese literary world is supposed to be shouldered by us. Here, I cannot help but cry out against this injustice!

Mr. Hunren said: "The creation of this abnormal phenomenon is the fault of the editors and bookstore owners, but the main reason is not entirely with them, but with the general blind readers, because they are a group of pitiful creatures without any prejudices, clinging to the purpose of the works of famous writers, and when literary giants say humorous writing is good, they read humorous magazines and books. When they say essays are good, they choose essays to read. In short, even a literary giant's fart smells fragrant to them. As for unknown works, they don't even bother to take a look, as if looking at them would cause them harm."

We believe that Mr. Hunren's remarks are too arbitrary and unfounded. It is true that famous writers are easier for us to notice because we are familiar with them, while unknown works are easily overlooked because they are too unfamiliar. Moreover, before we see them, we don't even know that there is a new person providing a good work somewhere. How can you ask us to pay attention in advance? In the current literary world, with no great works discovered and the daily impressions given to us by the real society being so bad, full of complaints and nowhere to vent our anger, humorous essays that give us a bit of laughter and scolding are naturally regarded as the only nourishment. To say that we are pitiful creatures without any prejudices, unable to distinguish good from bad, then let me ask, since the May Fourth Movement, how many new famous writers have emerged, like Mr. Hunren, who have joined the ranks of writers, and who recognized them? According to him, the reason why famous writers become famous is "by struggling with great, initially unknown works." Then who recognized these great, initially unknown works? We don't understand why Mr. Hunren's words are so contradictory.

As for saying that looking at unknown works would cause harm, the writers here don't understand the readers' difficulties. First, readers already find it very difficult to buy magazines, not to mention books. For example, the so-called "Special Issue for Unknown Writers" in the past wasted a lot of money, and the content was undoubtedly unqualified. This is in terms of economic ability. In terms of time, the time spent earning a living is already a whole day, with very little spare time. Many valuable books are still not free to explore. How can there be time to waste on disappointing results? This harm already exists primarily, not to mention anything else.

Passing Old Master Ridge

— Xicun

The horse pulling the cart, the people sitting lazily in the cart, were equally lazy. It was too hot. Encountering a westward road in the afternoon, the sun shone directly into the carriage from the arched front canopy, drenching both the lazy horse and the lazy people in sweat.

Along the way, there were hills and farmlands. It seemed as if the wind was completely blocked, but it was actually wrong to blame the wind. The trees in the mountains near and far were all drooping their heads so obviously, standing there blankly, which was clear evidence. So, fundamentally, there was no wind blowing this afternoon.

"We're almost at Old Master Ridge," said the coachman.

In Jilin Province alone, the number of mountain ridges named Old Master Ridge is probably more than the fingers on one hand. The Old Master Ridge mentioned here is located forty li southwest of Jilin Provincial City. In the past, before the South Manchuria Railway and the Jichang Railway were completed, anyone traveling from Shenyang to Jilin had to pass through this place because this road was the main post road.

Hearing the coachman say that we were approaching Old Master Ridge, the lazy passengers and those who were dozing off, bumping along with the cart, all sat up, grabbing the canopy bow, and invigorating their spirits, staring ahead with wide eyes. This was all because the ridge pass was a difficult obstacle.

This was the eastern ridge pass. From the bottom to the top of the ridge, it was at least three li long. Lush green trees grew on the roadside, and on the other side was a stone beach covered with chaotic rocks. A stream of spring water, no more than an inch deep, meandered across the stone beach. There were not many farmlands here, mostly forests, some tall, some short, and some weeds and wildflowers. There was also no one living here. Therefore, over the years, after the green gauze curtains rose, it became a nest for bandits to emerge.

The "Manchukuo's" maintenance of治安 was unmatched compared to the past. Encountering such places, travelers would naturally be worried.

"Old man, you have to keep your eyes open."

I think the coachman's words are useless. Even if your eyes can truly see in all directions and your ears can hear in all directions, please tell me, if you see and hear everything, can you escape the bullets from the bandits' guns? His appearance was really tense. In this situation, he was a hundred times more worried than us travelers because this cart was his entire property. If he encountered bandits and his horses were robbed, not only would his property be bankrupt, but it would also cut off his livelihood.

If at this time you heard a gunshot, or encountered five or six people loitering together, then everyone would be frightened. But we finally walked step by step to the top of the ridge.

To be honest, I am not afraid of bandits. I have nothing but my bare body. I would rather see them. Wouldn't it be even better if they were a small team of volunteer soldiers? A year ago, the anti-Japanese volunteer army had set up defenses here, which was indeed a dangerous place that soldiers had to fight for. I hope that in the near future, more of those heroic warriors will appear here again.

There is a temple at the top of the ridge. Except for the first and fifteenth days of the lunar month, when it is open, the two vermilion doors are always tightly closed. It is not easy to see the monks. Encountering such deep mountains, such dangerous places, such temples, one cannot help but think that there is a question mark there.

Opposite the temple is a steep cliff. The road passes through the middle, like a pass. The road going down the west side of the ridge is more difficult to walk than when climbing the ridge. Not only is the ridge road very steep, but it is also very narrow. This is the most difficult section to walk on the entire ridge. Sometimes, the horse pulling the shaft cannot steady its feet and slips, often overturning the cart. Then, the cart, the horse, and the coachman roll down the ridge like a pile of chaotic rocks.

Whenever going down the ridge, passengers always have to get out of the cart and walk until they reach the bottom of the mountain before they can sit down again.

In the evening, I stayed in a cart inn thirty li west of the ridge. I heard that a merchant carrying goods was robbed in the morning. The innkeeper said that there was a small gang on the ridge these days, with about five or six small guns. They don't rob carts, they don't rob poor guests. So, they are specifically paying attention to wealthy people. In that case, maybe they were hiding in the forest when we passed the ridge. Naturally, they saw us clearly. They didn't rob us, maybe they were kind enough to let us go?

The coachman, like a pardoned prisoner, drank old wine while smiling and asking us several passengers:

"Old men, we had good luck today. How about buying a few melons to eat after dinner?"

The innkeeper, as if he himself were a traveler, said with a smile, "This, of course, haha."

The passengers all smiled and reached into their pockets to take out money to complete this melon feast.

The Enemy That Bullets Cannot Eliminate

— American National Weekly

Planting Sweet Potatoes

— Pu Feng

Without enough land, the early rice was just harvested, and the plows and harrows immediately loosened the soil; without rest throughout the year, another season of sweet potatoes must be planted in the thin and barren fields.

The yellowish-black soil was hooked up, and long soil ridges cleared deep and long paths. Sweet potato seedlings more than a foot long were put down, a thin layer of fertilizer was spread, and another layer of soil was immediately added.

The seedlings were constantly planted, the ashes were continuously spread, and the soil was constantly piled up; how many sweat drops were buried by the hoe each time? How much hard work did each sweet potato seedling accumulate?

The withered seedlings clung tightly to the soil, and bucket after bucket of water was poured down, also hoping for rain and dew from the heavens. Yes, perhaps the green leaves will show vitality tomorrow, but who guarantees that there will definitely be a good harvest three months later?

Psychological Calligraphy Expert Infers Good and Bad Fortune

— Wu Shaoxi

I remember that three or four months ago, scientific spirit writing diagrams were all the rage in Shanghai. At that time, all the newspapers attacked them fiercely, thinking that it was right to drive out superstition and ghosts borrowing the name of science to do strange things there.

Unexpectedly, as time passed, the ghosts of scientific spirit writing had just been driven out, and a very beautiful American professor came again, who was the psychological calligraphy expert Professor Ren Dao (Prof. Zandar), who can look at a person's handwriting and infer their past and future. He is now stationed in a certain hotel and officially meets the people of Shanghai, and can infer the good and bad fortune of love, marriage, wealth, career, and travel, so that people know what to pursue and avoid.

This matter can attract people's attention, because Mr. Ren Dao is a professor, a psychological calligraphy expert, so naturally he is a scientist, and his inferences are certainly more "scientific" and more effective than scientific spirit writing.

However, the facts that psychology tells us are different from this. Although a few psychologists also study calligraphy, they only want to infer a person's personality from the handwriting, and can never investigate good or bad fortune. This kind of research is still in its infancy, has not reached maturity, and has not obtained any completely reliable conclusions. Some psychologists even doubt the possibility of success of this kind of research. But now there are people who are fueling the flames beyond the scope and ability of psychology, thinking that good and bad fortune can be inferred from calligraphy. What an absurd thing this is.

It is very obvious that professor and psychological calligraphy expert are deceptive titles, and in reality it is just a genuine江湖客 — foreigners' tricks are after all fresher than those of Chinese people, and江湖 fortune-telling combined with a professor, plus commercialized biscuits, the three are not worried about not matching the taste of Shanghai people, or many people will want to be anesthetized once, but psychology will suffer.

Younger Brother (12)

— Zhou Wen

When I ran into their brigade headquarters, his colleagues told me that he had been sent to escort things to the provincial capital and lost them and would be back tomorrow. Those colleagues had known for a long time that I was going to Nanjing and thought that I would definitely have a lot of influence in the future. They all came to curry favor with me, saying that they were all good friends of my younger brother. They said that my younger brother was very small, and people bullied him. He had even been beaten by a company commander. He seemed very negative.

The next day, while I was still in my younger brother's bed, I heard someone calling "Older brother" in my ear. When I opened my eyes, I almost didn't recognize him as my younger brother. Although his face was still as black as before, it was very thin, and his cheekbones seemed about to protrude. His face was no longer as rugged as before, but had a deep complexion. He looked at me as if he was very happy, but he couldn't speak.

"Younger brother, I've been waiting for you for a day," I said, sitting up and grabbing his hand.

"Yes, I rushed back."

"Younger brother, you..."

Just then, a colleague walked in, and my younger brother suddenly winked at me, as if implying that I shouldn't rush to speak. He urged me to wash my face and come out with him.

On the road, my younger brother looked left and right before saying:

"Did those guys talk to you about anything?"

"We talked, just casually. They said they were all your good friends."

"Humph, good friends! They almost killed me. Older brother, after you leave, I must come in the future. This kind of thing is really not for humans, it's despicable and disgusting!"

Just as he was talking, my younger brother's shoulder was suddenly patted heavily, followed by a voice:

"Where are you going!"

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Questions on Reading "Accepting the Legacy and Sorting Out the National Past"

— A Long

Yesterday, I happened to have an urgent need and went to the toilet. I happened to have the book "Literature, Volume 3, Number 3" with me, so I carefully read it in the toilet. When I read the article "Accepting the Legacy and Sorting Out the National Past," I found a few doubts, but I have very few friends who are writers who accept the legacy, so I have no way to ask for advice. I have to write it out again to ask for advice from writers who have accepted the literary legacy, hoping that Mr. Hua Sheng will not misunderstand again and say that I am writing 洋八股 and have ulterior motives.

Here, I must first declare that I am not writing this article to participate in the battle group, nor am I deliberately messing up the solemn literary world. Most of the writers in the literary world are friends with deep roots and are very remarkable. Therefore, although I don't treat the articles of writers in the literary world like Christians treat the Bible as a sword, I also value them like our country's Bible-like biographies. How dare I participate in and mess up the literary world.

I started reading the first sentence, "Since the beginning of this year, this journal has raised the issue of literary legacy." I was shocked and deeply sorry, "Literary legacy" was originally proposed by your journal first, which is as valuable as Watt's invention of steam and Columbus's discovery of the New World. Some people say that this term is imported from "Russia," but in any case, it is a treasure that the gentleman has painstakingly accepted from foreign countries as a literary legacy, but this will not be discussed.

But what I don't understand is the word "legacy." If according to my stupid explanation, assuming that the ancestors are dead, the property left behind is called "legacy." The literary explanation is probably no exception, but between the literary ancestors' death and the general filial descendants' acceptance of the legacy, there must be a period of time. I don't know in which year the death of our country's literary ancestors occurred? And I don't know in which month the inheritors accepted the "literary legacy"? I really don't understand it at all.

If according to the political system, is the establishment of the Republic of China the beginning of the "accepting the literary legacy" period, or is the establishment of the National Government the beginning of the "accepting the literary legacy" period? If according to the literary system, is the abolition of the imperial examination the beginning of the "accepting the literary legacy" period, or is the vernacular movement the beginning of the "accepting the literary legacy" period? Or is the shouting of the masses' language the beginning of the "accepting the literary legacy" period? Where is the "paragraph" period in between?

There is also one point, what is the difference between "literary legacy" and "sorting out the national past"? According to Mr. Hua, "So we raise the issue of the Chinese literary legacy, not to actively indicate what the legacy is, but to passively point out what is not the legacy." According to Mr. Lin Xiao, "What is the difference between 'literary legacy' and 'sorting out the national past'?" According to the two gentlemen, although the names are different, the nature is not much different. But I approve of the four characters "sorting out the national past." Why? If you look at the literal meaning of the four characters "literary legacy," "literary legacy" is to accept all the ancestors' literature, but among the legacy, gold, silver, and jewelry are naturally accepted, but broken tables, broken benches, and broken rags are also accepted at the same time, without any distinction or choice. Unless Mr. Hua comes to explain like Master Zhu's notes, we are really ignorant.

If you say "sorting out the national past," since it has been sorted out, of course there is the meaning of re-allocation, distinguishing between what to take and what to leave. Among the national past, some of course should be displayed in the museum, some should be displayed in the libraries of various provinces, preparing for people from various places who study academics to refer to, and some should be placed in the public education hall for everyone to study. This is the meaning of "sorting out the national past," which the Western philosophers call re-criticism and re-evaluation. And Mr. Hua must say that "literary legacy" is right, and "sorting out the national past" is wrong. If it's not that the gentleman has ulterior motives (borrowing the gentleman's words), what other reason is there?

There is another question, Mr. Hua said: "Chu Ci is the name of a general collection, and Lisao is just one of them, and it shouldn't be said so confusedly." My view of these two sentences is also somewhat different from the gentleman's. When I was more than ten years old, a Mr. Li wearing old-fashioned glasses told me about the biographies of Qu Yuan, saying, "Qu Yuan was worried that the king was not intelligent, that slander covered the light, that evil harmed the public, and that justice was not welcome, so he made Lisao out of worry and contemplation." When Mr. Li talked about this, he pushed his glasses up to his forehead and scolded the foolish monarch loudly, and he turned around and solemnly told me that you should not misunderstand, the so-called "Lisao" does not only refer to the Lisao article, but refers to the entire Lisao collection of Qu Yuan, because Lisao is the first article, so the entire book is named after Lisao, and later people called it Chu Ci, because Qu Yuan was from the state of Chu, so it is called Chu Ci, but in fact Chu Ci is not limited to the book Lisao, that is, such as Song Yu, Tang Le, and Jing Cha are all Chu people, so their works are also included in it. The entire Lisao collection is named Lisao, just like the first two characters in the first sentence of "Xue Er Ba Yi" are used as the general name of the entire book. This is what I heard from my teacher.

Later, I also came to study this sentence a little bit myself. Since it is said, "Therefore, he made Lisao out of worry and contemplation," it can be known that it is not only the Lisao article, but what Qu Yuan made out of worry and contemplation, and the other articles were not made out of Qu Yuan's worry and contemplation, the meaning is very clear. Try to observe the following "Tai Shi Gong said, I read Lisao, Tianwen, Zhaohun, Aiying, and was saddened by his ambition," then the following articles are also undoubtedly made out of worry and contemplation, so later people even annotated this sentence as Tianwen, Zhaohun, Aiying in Lisao. Although the saying is not necessarily true, it is also passable. And Mr. Hua must say that Chu Ci is the name of a general collection, and Lisao is an article in the general collection. Since his advocacy is so firm and his explanation is so clear, because I have not accepted Qu Yuan's literary legacy, I dare not argue. Perhaps the old-fashioned gentlemen in the past are unreliable, or perhaps Tai Shi Gong is also a gentleman who heard well and saw plainly, and did not accept Mr. Qu Yuan's literary legacy, so there is this misunderstanding? This is also my question.

In short, in a unified way, foreign imports are reliable, and the four characters of literary legacy, no matter how you mix them up, the head size always fits, and readers feel new and joyful when they read it. If you say sorting out the national past, I have a headache when I hear it. I advise the two gentlemen, Mingtang and Lin Xiao, to read more books and not to talk nonsense.

Autumn Memories

— Ms. Jiong

Autumn is here!

The unprecedented heat of the past sixty years has disappeared without a trace and will no longer grow in this world.

Although the refreshing weather makes people feel comfortable, a sad mood cannot help but float up a layer of melancholy!

The wind blows in gusts, and the breath of infinite coolness comfortably invades the naive heart of childhood. Chrysanthemums are blooming in various colors, yellow, white, and different colors. Butterflies fly in pairs in the dense chrysanthemum bushes.

Autumn is here, and many crickets are buried in the flowers and plants, constantly making autumn sounds, implicitly tempting us to pursue their traces. The clear blue pond is quiet and beautiful. The autumn wind blows, causing ripples, and the willow branches are reflected in the water. Our fishing boats float and dance on the water. At that time, I was seven years old and my brother Jing was five years old. I vaguely remember that autumn. My father ran to the provincial capital for official business and did not return for three years! My mother was almost exhausted from the busyness of my older sister's wedding, unable to rest day or night! Our whole family said that autumn was an unprecedented season! Only my brother Jing and I, without any evil intentions, still lived a life of indifference! Every day, we always took advantage of the arrival of autumn, when there was no strong sunlight shining on our heads, we would hide in the bamboo forest and grope for the origin of the autumn insects that were calling 喞喞. We hunted crickets everywhere, but when the crickets heard human voices, they stopped calling and quietly hid.

This year's autumn has arrived as expected.

Page 23

The shadows of the trees are sparsely reflected on the window, and the flowers and plants become so withered and yellow overnight. The evening wind blows, and the crickets seem to have disappeared. In the eight years that I have drifted in this dusty city, I have never heard their sad cry again! With the flowing years, the scenes of childhood have all dissipated in the years of chaos between soldiers and bandits in my hometown, and can never be presented before my eyes again.

The autumn moon gushes out a crystal clear plain color, as if it can connect all souls and become the vast universe. The autumn tong trees hit the surroundings of the house, and together with the autumn wind, they hit the leaves, making rustling sounds. Following the shadows of autumn, the happy childhood heart has long been buried so quietly by frequent sorrows. If I could hear some autumn insects chirping from the courtyard of my childhood, I think my heart would also be the same, only slightly depressed.

Autumn Window Musings, One

— Jun

—The Jasmine-Selling Girl—

Following several days of rain, a tender coolness of autumn shrouded the human world.

Autumn brings some pleasures that the just-departed height of summer lacked, allowing the suppressed breaths, soaked in the west wind for months, to ease a little; but at the same time, it also brings some faint melancholy, lacking in the height of summer, and a concentrated sadness. Although the heat lingers, reminiscent of the departed summer, it newly adds a thick layer of melancholic feeling to the mind.

The autumn of the season and the autumn of the heart, ah!

Perhaps there are still green leaves to be longed for in autumn. However, before my eyes, an endless grayness is spread out as if a net. I feel that everything outside me has gradually detached itself from me, becoming ever colder and more distant, leaving me living alone in the crowded island of humanity.

"Autumn has come again, oh, the heart of a wanderer!" I often murmur this towards the gloomy, leaden sky. After a period of murmuring, a feeling, also like a lump of copper, presses upon my heart. Every day, I hear the clamorous shouts on the street in the alley below, and among those shouting voices, there is a sighing voice like that of a young woman, "Jasmine flowers for sale, jasmine flowers for sale," crisply entering my ears, and I can't help but echo in my heart in the same tone:

"Autumn jasmine flowers, oh, the heart of a wanderer!"

Sighing so deeply.

That young woman selling jasmine flowers, although having the youth of a jasmine flower, no longer has the fresh and beautiful color of a jasmine flower's youth. Dim, like a jasmine flower left overnight, about to wither.

After calling out a few times, she disappears into the noisy clamor. But after the calling sound passes, a silent sound remains on my heart, lingering, along with the shadow of a youthful yet haggard figure.

But it has been a full year since I saw that shadow or heard that sighing voice!

But this shadow and this silent sound also eternally gnaw at my thoughts, like a worm, until this day.

And afterwards, every day I still lean against the small window, watching the sunlight shine on the high wall opposite, and then sink down in the afternoon. Everything is unchanged, except that the sound and the shadow are gone. Sometimes when I accidentally think of it, I look at the clouds drifting leisurely across the sky, the azure sky, immersed in a deep and long memory, already a year has passed.

Now, the sun rises straight and sets early, it is autumn.

The young woman selling autumn jasmine flowers appears again, unharmed, between these alleys and long streets. Still the more sighing voice, and the more haggard shadow.

Autumn has aged her once again.

Hearing that sighing voice, my wanderer's feeling becomes heavier. I feel a kind of gossamer-like, light smoke of melancholy, faintly twining around my heart: my entire soul. And from there, I long for a small, sad soul. Following me, a wanderer, living alone, passing the days in silence.

Hearing that sighing voice, I am saddened by the alienation between people, while at the same time, I feel the intimate taste of being misunderstood by others as a lonely person.

Autumn goes and comes again, comes and goes again. Sending off countless autumns in this way, listening to the chirping of crickets and the sound of falling leaves on autumn days, the sunset bell of my own life has passed by delicately, passed by.

The landlord said: "It's that it doesn't rain, what does it have to do with me!"

Side View of Autumn

— Huiren

In the factory, the whistle, in the quiet autumn morning, howls wildly, breaking through the black sky, penetrating the layers of increasingly white clouds in the treetops to the east; the morning breeze blows on the flat, shining asphalt road, stirring the leaves falling from the plane trees, the sound is unusually weak.

People shrinking their necks, dragging their heavy steps with a lack of energy, step on the leaves quickly, yet weakly, heading towards the place emitting black smoke. A piece of drowsy-seeming weariness still covers people's faces; when a branch of dim light shoots down from the treetops, they close their eyes as if unable to resist; yellow like a carved plaster statue, almost having lost their emotions; the women's heads still retain the mark of last night's labor, a thin layer of yellowish fluff, enough to show that their time is rushed, not allowing for the slightest opportunity to tidy up and adorn themselves.

Stepping onto the ferry, one feels the silence of the world, the coldness of the surging river water, the coolness of the river wind blowing on the face, almost everything is like death. In the silence, thoughts surge in people's minds, chewing over the dreams they haven't finished yet, and estimating their own lives; but these, which always become questions in people's minds, only turn into a kind of nameless anger, surging like the morning tide.

They are aware that autumn has arrived! A cruel, ruthless, and also angry season, they cannot see the other side of autumn, the side that is gentle; joyful, moving; just as the people of that side of autumn cannot see the coldness, ruthlessness, and anger of autumn.

They are forever separated, as if by an iron wall.

When Lonely

— Lu Yin Quan

Arriving in Nanjing, like a dried-up well, my heart became as desolate as a dried-up well. Hiding in a small attic room, immersed in the overflowing dim light, I feel strangely lonely, what shall I do? In the past, I used to be very fond of solitude, because its faint sweetness was indeed enough for one to savor carefully; but now, I not only do not enjoy
